SELECT T0."BaseRef",       T1."ContraAct",       CASE WHEN T2."AcctName" <> ''  THEN   T2."AcctName"       ELSE T3."CardName" END AS "Descrição da operação",       T1."Debit",       T1."Credit",       T1."BPLName",       T1."RefDate",       T1."LineMemo",       T1."Account",              CASE            WHEN  T1."Debit">0 THEN 'DEBITO'            WHEN  T1."Credit">0 THEN 'CREDITO'       END AS "Tipo de operação",        CASE            WHEN T0."TransType" = 46 THEN 'Contas a pagar'            WHEN T0."TransType" = 30 THEN 'LCM'            WHEN T0."TransType" = 24 THEN 'Contas a receber'       END AS "Tipo de documento gerador"        FROM OJDT T0 INNER JOIN JDT1 T1 ON T0."TransId" = T1."TransId" LEFT JOIN OACT T2 ON  T1."ContraAct"= T2."AcctCode" LEFT JOIN OCRD T3 ON T3."CardCode" = T1."ContraAct" LEFT JOIN OUSR T4 ON T4."USERID" = T0."UserSign" WHERE T1."ShortName" in ('2.01.01.03.18','2.01.01.03.14','2.01.01.03.15','2.01.01.03.16','2.01.01.03.17','1.01.03.08.07','1.01.03.08.05','1.01.03.08.06','1.01.03.08.07','1.01.03.08.08','1.01.03.08.09','2.01.01.11.21','2.01.01.11.22','2.01.01.11.23','2.01.01.11.24','2.01.01.11.25','2.01.01.11.26','2.01.01.11.27')  and T0."TransType" in (46,30,24) AND T1."RefDate" >= [%4] AND T1."RefDate"<=[%5]  AND T0."TransId" NOT IN (SELECT T0."StornoToTr"  FROM OJDT T0 WHERE T0."StornoToTr" IS NOT NULL)  AND T0."StornoToTr" IS NULL  AND T1."LineMemo" NOT LIKE 'Retorno%%' ORDER BY T0."BaseRef" ASC;

-- - Título: Relatorio de contra notas e seus preços - (0293)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de contra notas e seus preços - (0293).
WITH cte as (SELECT T0."DocNum",T0."LogInstanc", T0."DocDate", T0."DocDueDate" AS "Data de entrega",T0."BPLId",T3."BPLName",T0."CardCode", T0."CardName", T6."U_NAME",T1."LineNum", T2."ItemCode", T2."ItemName",T5."ItmsGrpNam",T0."DiscPrcnt" as "Desconto_documento", T1."DiscPrcnt" as "Desconto_linha",T1."Quantity", T1."PriceBefDi", T1."LineTotal", T1."WhsCode",T1."LogInstanc"  as "Linha_log" , 'HISTORICO' AS "ATUAL"   FROM ADOC T0   INNER JOIN ADO1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" AND T1."ObjType" = 22 INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode"  LEFT JOIN OBPL T3 ON T3."BPLId" = T0."BPLId"  LEFT JOIN OITM T4 ON T4."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITB T5 ON T5."ItmsGrpCod" = T4."ItmsGrpCod" LEFT JOIN OUSR T6 ON T0."UserSign2" = T6."INTERNAL_K"  WHERE T0."ObjType" =22 AND T0."CANCELED" ='N'  AND T1."LogInstanc" = 1 )   SELECT  T12."TaxDate",  T12."DocDate", T0."DocNum" as "Nro PEDIDO" ,  T12."Serial" as "Nro NF", T4."Usage",  T3."ItemCode",  T3."ItemName",  T5."ItmsGrpNam", CASE WHEN T0."DocStatus" ='O' THEN 'ABERTO' ELSE 'FECHADO' END AS "Status Doc" , T1."Quantity" as "Quantidade Pedido",  T11."Quantity" as "Quantidade NF" ,  CASE WHEN T1."Quantity">T11."Quantity" THEN 'Quantidade do Pedido MAIOR' WHEN T1."Quantity"<T11."Quantity" THEN 'Quantidade da NF MAIOR' ELSE 'OK' END AS "Analise_quantidade", T13."Quantity" AS "Quantidade NF Devolução" ,  T6."CardCode",  T6."CardName",  T7."BPLName", COALESCE((SELECT min(T00."PriceBefDi") FROM cte T00 WHERE T00."DocNum" = T0."DocNum" AND T00."LineNum" = T1."LineNum" AND T00."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode" ),T1."PriceBefDi")  as "Primeiro preço Pedido"  , T1."PriceBefDi" as "Preço Pedido", CASE WHEN T1."PriceBefDi">(SELECT max(T00."PriceBefDi") FROM cte T00 WHERE T00."DocNum" = T0."DocNum" AND T00."LineNum" = T1."LineNum" AND T00."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode" )THEN 'Preço do Pedido atual MAIOR que HISTORICO'  WHEN T1."PriceBefDi"<(SELECT max(T00."PriceBefDi") FROM cte T00 WHERE T00."DocNum" = T0."DocNum" AND T00."LineNum" = T1."LineNum" AND T00."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode" )THEN 'Preço do Pedido atual MENOR que HISTORICO' ELSE 'OK' END AS  "Analise Preço pedido atual X 1° HISTORICO", T11."PriceBefDi" as "Preço NF", CASE WHEN T1."PriceBefDi">T11."PriceBefDi" THEN 'Preço do Pedido MAIOR' WHEN T1."PriceBefDi"<T11."PriceBefDi" THEN 'Preço da NF MAIOR' ELSE 'OK' END AS  "Analise_preco", T13."PriceBefDi" as "Preço NF devolucao"  FROM OPOR T0   INNER JOIN POR1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OITM T3 ON T1."ItemCode" = T3."ItemCode"  LEFT JOIN OUSG T4 ON T1."Usage" = T4."ID"  LEFT JOIN OITB T5 ON T3."ItmsGrpCod" = T5."ItmsGrpCod"  LEFT JOIN OCRD T6 ON T0."CardCode" = T6."CardCode"  LEFT JOIN OBPL T7 ON T0."BPLId" = T7."BPLId"  LEFT JOIN OSLP T8 ON T0."SlpCode" = T8."SlpCode" LEFT JOIN PDN1 T9 ON TO_VARCHAR(T9."BaseRef") = TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum") and TO_VARCHAR(T9."BaseLine") = TO_VARCHAR(T1."LineNum") LEFT JOIN OPDN T10 ON T10."DocEntry"  = T9."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN PCH1 T11 ON TO_VARCHAR(T11."BaseRef")  = TO_VARCHAR(T10."DocNum")  AND T11."BaseLine"  = T9."LineNum" AND T11."BaseType" = 20 LEFT JOIN OPCH T12 ON T12."DocEntry" = T11."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN RPC1 T13 ON TO_VARCHAR(T13."BaseRef") =TO_VARCHAR(T12."DocNum") AND T13."BaseLine" = T11."LineNum"  LEFT JOIN ORPC T14 ON T14."DocEntry" = T13."DocEntry"   WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T12."DocDate">=[%1]  AND T12."DocDate"<=[%2]   AND (T10."CANCELED" ='N' OR T10."CANCELED" IS NULL) AND   (T12."CANCELED" ='N' OR T12."CANCELED" IS NULL) AND T12."SeqCode" NOT IN (42,1,-2,38,39,-1);

-- - Título: Relatorio de ctes e seus locais de saida e entrega - (0289)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de ctes e seus locais de saida e entrega - (0289).
SELECT  DISTINCT  T0."DocNum",  T0."DocDate",  T0."TaxDate", T0."CardCode", T0."CardName",  T6."BPLName", T7."BaseRef" as "Nro PEDIDO", T0."Serial", T0."DocTotal",   T2."Name" AS "Estado Saida de mercadorias",  T4."Name" as "Municipio Saida de mercadorias",   T3."Name" AS "Estado Local de entrega",  T5."Name" as "Municipio Local de entrega", T0."Comments"  FROM OPCH T0   INNER JOIN PCH12 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"   LEFT JOIN OCST T2 ON T1."StateGIP"= T2."Code" LEFT JOIN OCST T3 ON T1."StatDlvryP"= T3."Code"  LEFT JOIN OCNT T4 ON TO_VARCHAR(T1."CountyGIP") = TO_VARCHAR(T4."AbsId" ) LEFT JOIN OCNT T5 ON TO_VARCHAR(T1."CntyDlvryP") = TO_VARCHAR(T5."AbsId" ) LEFT JOIN OBPL T6 ON T6."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" LEFT JOIN PCH1 T7 ON T7."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry"     WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."Model" = 45 AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] ORDER BY T0."CardCode", T0."DocNum";

-- - Título: Relatorio de custo de MP unidade de medida (TERESÓPOLIS) - (0162)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de custo de mp unidade de medida (teresópolis) - (0162).
SELECT  T1."ItemCode", T2."ItemName", T2."BuyUnitMsr", T3."ItmsGrpNam",  SUM(T1."Quantity") AS "Quantidade", SUM (T1."LineTotal") as "Valor R$",  SUM (T1."LineTotal")/ SUM(T1."Quantity")  AS "Preço médio R$ Unid. Medida de compra."   FROM OPCH T0   INNER JOIN PCH1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode"  INNER JOIN OITB T3 ON T2."ItmsGrpCod" = T3."ItmsGrpCod"  WHERE T0."BPLId" in (3,4,6,10) AND T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."U_NotaAjusteInterno" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T1."Usage" in (19,47) AND T3."ItmsGrpCod" IN (119,120,122,123,124,125,131)   GROUP BY T1."ItemCode", T2."ItemName",T2."BuyUnitMsr",T3."ItmsGrpNam" ORDER BY T3."ItmsGrpNam", T2."ItemName";

-- - Título: Relatorio de depesas de importação lançadas - (0211)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de depesas de importação lançadas - (0211).
SELECT T0."DocNum", T0."DocDate", T0."CardCode", T0."SuppName", T0."DocTotal", T0."CostSum", T1."ItemCode", T1."Dscription", T1."Quantity", T1."Cost" AS "Despesa por unidade R$", (SELECT T00."DocNum" FROM OPDN T00 WHERE T00."DocEntry" = T1."BaseEntry") AS "Nro do recebimento" , (SELECT T00."DocDate" FROM OPDN T00 WHERE T00."DocEntry" = T1."BaseEntry") as "Data do recebimento", 'Recebimento' as "Tipo do doc"  FROM OIPF T0  INNER JOIN IPF1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry";

-- - Título: Relatorio de despesas e devolução compra manoel - (0328)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de despesas e devolução compra manoel - (0328).
SELECT     T0."DocNum",     T10."NfmName" AS "Modelo",     T0."DocDate",     T0."Serial" AS "Número nota fiscal",     T0."CardCode",     T0."CardName",     T0."DocTotal",     T1."BPLName",     T0."DocTotal",     'COMPRA' AS "TIPO",      T2."LineNum",     COALESCE(T2."ItemCode", T5."AcctCode") AS "Codigo do item/Conta",     COALESCE(T4."ItemName", T5."AcctName") AS "Nome do item/Conta",     T2."PriceBefDi",     T2."Quantity",     T2."LineTotal",     T3."Usage",    STRING_AGG(     CASE          WHEN T01."Debit" > 0          THEN T01."Account"     END,     ' | '   ) AS "Codigos contas movimentadas A DEBITO",    STRING_AGG(     CASE          WHEN T01."Debit" > 0          THEN T01."Account" || ' ' || T02."AcctName"     END,     ' | '   ) AS "Contas movimentadas A DEBITO", STRING_AGG(     CASE          WHEN T01."Credit" > 0          THEN T01."Account"      END,     ' | ' ) AS "Codigos contas movimentadas A CREDITO", STRING_AGG(     CASE          WHEN T01."Credit" > 0          THEN T01."Account" || ' ' || T02."AcctName"     END,     ' | ' ) AS "Contas movimentadas A CREDITO" FROM OPCH T0 INNER JOIN OBPL T1     ON T0."BPLId" = T1."BPLId" LEFT JOIN PCH1 T2     ON T2."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OUSG T3     ON T3."ID" = T2."Usage" LEFT JOIN OITM T4     ON T4."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OACT T5     ON T5."AcctCode" = T2."AcctCode" LEFT JOIN OJDT T00 ON  TO_VARCHAR(T00."BaseRef") = TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum") AND T00."TransType" = 18 LEFT JOIN JDT1 T01 ON T00."TransId" = T01."TransId"  LEFT JOIN OACT T02 ON T02."AcctCode" = T01."Account" LEFT JOIN ONFM T10 ON T0."Model" = T10."AbsEntry"  WHERE T0."CANCELED" = 'N'  AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2]    AND T0."BPLId" IN (9,6) GROUP BY      T0."DocNum",     T0."DocDate",     T10."NfmName",     T0."Serial",     T0."CardCode",     T0."CardName",     T0."DocTotal",     T1."BPLName",     T0."DocTotal", T2."LineNum",     COALESCE(T2."ItemCode", T5."AcctCode"),     COALESCE(T4."ItemName", T5."AcctName"),     T2."PriceBefDi",     T2."Quantity",     T2."LineTotal",     T3."Usage"  UNION ALL  SELECT     T0."DocNum",     T10."NfmName",     T0."DocDate",     T0."Serial" AS "Número nota fiscal",     T0."CardCode",     T0."CardName",     T0."DocTotal",     T1."BPLName",     T0."DocTotal",     'DEVOLUÇÃO DE COMPRA' AS "TIPO", T2."LineNum",     COALESCE(T2."ItemCode", T5."AcctCode") AS "Codigo do item/Conta",     COALESCE(T4."ItemName", T5."AcctName") AS "Nome do item/Conta",     T2."PriceBefDi",     T2."Quantity",     T2."LineTotal",     T3."Usage",    STRING_AGG(     CASE          WHEN T01."Debit" > 0          THEN T01."Account"     END,     ' | '   ) AS "Codigos contas movimentadas A DEBITO", STRING_AGG(     CASE          WHEN T01."Debit" > 0          THEN T01."Account" || ' ' || T02."AcctName"     END,     ' | ' ) AS "Contas movimentadas A DEBITO", STRING_AGG(     CASE          WHEN T01."Credit" > 0          THEN T01."Account"      END,     ' | ' ) AS "Codigos contas movimentadas A CREDITO", STRING_AGG(     CASE          WHEN T01."Credit" > 0          THEN T01."Account" || ' ' || T02."AcctName"     END,     ' | ' ) AS "Contas movimentadas A CREDITO" FROM ORPC T0 INNER JOIN OBPL T1     ON T0."BPLId" = T1."BPLId" LEFT JOIN RPC1 T2     ON T2."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OUSG T3     ON T3."ID" = T2."Usage" LEFT JOIN OITM T4     ON T4."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OACT T5     ON T5."AcctCode" = T2."AcctCode" LEFT JOIN OJDT T00 ON  TO_VARCHAR(T00."BaseRef") = TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum") AND T00."TransType" = 19 LEFT JOIN JDT1 T01 ON T00."TransId" = T01."TransId" LEFT JOIN OACT T02 ON T02."AcctCode" = T01."Account" LEFT JOIN ONFM T10 ON T0."Model" = T10."AbsEntry" WHERE T0."CANCELED" = 'N'   AND T0."BPLId" IN (9,6) AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2]   GROUP BY      T0."DocNum",     T10."NfmName",     T0."DocDate",     T0."Serial",     T0."CardCode",     T0."CardName",     T0."DocTotal",     T1."BPLName",     T0."DocTotal",     T2."LineNum",     COALESCE(T2."ItemCode", T5."AcctCode"),     COALESCE(T4."ItemName", T5."AcctName"),     T2."PriceBefDi",     T2."Quantity",     T2."LineTotal",     T3."Usage";

-- - Título: Relatorio de devolução - frutas - RECIFE - (0308)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de devolução - frutas - recife - (0308).
SELECT T0."DocNum", T0."Serial", T0."DocDate", T0."CardCode", T0."CardName", T5."Name" as "Rede comercial",T6."Name" as "Rede CR",T7."BPLName", T0."DocTotal",  T2."ItemCode", T2."ItemName", T4."ItmsGrpNam", T1."Quantity", T1."PriceBefDi", T1."LineTotal" FROM ORIN T0   INNER JOIN RIN1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode"  LEFT JOIN OCRD T3 ON T0."CardCode" = T3."CardCode"  LEFT JOIN OITB T4 ON T2."ItmsGrpCod" = T4."ItmsGrpCod" LEFT JOIN "@SD_CADREDE" T5 ON T5."Code" = T3."U_SD_Rede" LEFT JOIN "@DE_PARA_CR" T6 ON T6."Code" = T0."CardCode"  INNER JOIN OBPL T7 ON T0."BPLId" = T7."BPLId" WHERE T1."Usage" in (15,74) AND T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."BPLId" in (1,9) AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate" <=[%2] and T4."ItmsGrpCod"  =131;

-- - Título: Relatorio de devolução CP - auditoria - (0307)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de devolução cp - auditoria - (0307).
WITH    cte AS (     SELECT        DISTINCT T2."ReconDate",        T0."CANCELED",        T0."DocEntry",        T0."DocNum",        T0."CardCode",        T11."CardName",        T0."Serial",        T10."BPLName",        T0."DocDate",        T0."DocTotal",        T1."ReconSum",         T2."ReconType",       CASE WHEN T2."ReconType" = 4 THEN 'Gerado nota de devolucao' WHEN T2."ReconType" = 3 THEN 'Baixa CP' WHEN T2."ReconType" = 0 THEN 'Nota reconciliada' END AS "Status",        T2."ReconDate" AS "Data contábil de fechamento da nota fiscal",        T0."DocStatus",        CASE WHEN T0."DocStatus" = 'O'        AND T2."CreateDate" IS NOT NULL AND T2."ReconType" <>13 THEN 'SALDO PARCIAL UTILIZADO' WHEN T0."DocStatus" = 'C'        AND T2."CreateDate" IS NOT NULL THEN 'FECHADO' END AS "NOTA FOI RECONCILIADA",        T5."DocDate" AS "Data_da_baixa",        T0."DocDueDate",        T5."DocNum" AS "DocNumContasAReceber",        T2."ReconNum" AS "DocNumReconciliacao",        T2."UserSign" AS "CodUsuario",        CASE WHEN T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido" = 'N' THEN 'NÃO' ELSE 'SIM' END AS "U_SDCanhotoRecebido",        T12."U_NAME"      FROM        ORPC T0        LEFT JOIN ITR1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."SrcObjAbs"        AND T1."SrcObjTyp" = 19       AND T1."ReconNum" NOT IN (         SELECT            T00."ReconNum"          FROM            OITR T00          WHERE            (             T00."Canceled" = 'Y'              or T00."ReconType" = 7           )       )        LEFT JOIN OITR T2 ON T1."ReconNum" = T2."ReconNum"        AND (         T2."Canceled" = 'N'          OR T2."Canceled" IS NULL       )        LEFT JOIN "@DE_PARA_CR" T4 ON T4."Code" = T0."CardCode"        LEFT JOIN VPM2 T3 ON T3."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry"        AND T3."DocNum" NOT IN (         SELECT            T00."DocEntry"          FROM            ORCT T00          WHERE            T00."Canceled" = 'Y'       )  AND T3."SumApplied" = T1."ReconSum"        AND T3."InvType" = 19       LEFT JOIN OVPM T5 ON T5."DocEntry" = T3."DocNum"  AND T2."ReconDate" = T5."DocDate"        AND T5."Canceled" = 'N'        AND T2."ReconType" = 3        LEFT JOIN OCRD T6 ON T6."CardCode" = T0."CardCode"        LEFT JOIN OCTG T7 ON T6."GroupNum" = T7."GroupNum"        LEFT JOIN INV1 T8 ON T8."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry"        LEFT JOIN OITM T9 ON T9."ItemCode" = T8."ItemCode"        LEFT JOIN OBPL T10 ON T10."BPLId" = T0."BPLId"        LEFT JOIN OCRD T11 ON T11."CardCode" = T0."CardCode"        LEFT JOIN OUSR T12 ON T12."INTERNAL_K" = T2."UserSign"      WHERE        (         T0."CANCELED" IN ('N', 'Y')       )        AND T2."ReconDate" >= [%1]        AND T2."ReconDate"  <= [%2]   )  SELECT    DISTINCT T00."ReconDate",    T00."CANCELED",    T00."DocEntry",    T00."DocNum",    T00."CardCode",    T00."CardName",    T00."Serial",    T00."BPLName",    T00."DocDate",    T00."Status",  T00."ReconType",   T00."DocTotal",    T00."ReconSum",    T00."Data contábil de fechamento da nota fiscal",    T00."DocStatus",    T00."NOTA FOI RECONCILIADA",    T00."Data_da_baixa",    T00."DocDueDate",    T00."DocNumContasAReceber",    T00."DocNumReconciliacao",    T00."CodUsuario",    T00."U_SDCanhotoRecebido",    T00."U_NAME"  FROM    cte T00  GROUP BY    T00."ReconDate",    T00."CANCELED",    T00."DocEntry",    T00."DocNum",    T00."CardCode",    T00."CardName",    T00."Serial",    T00."BPLName",    T00."DocDate",    T00."Status",  T00."ReconType",   T00."DocTotal",    T00."ReconSum",    T00."Data contábil de fechamento da nota fiscal",    T00."DocStatus",    T00."NOTA FOI RECONCILIADA",    T00."Data_da_baixa",    T00."DocDueDate",    T00."DocNumContasAReceber",    T00."DocNumReconciliacao",    T00."CodUsuario",    T00."U_SDCanhotoRecebido",    T00."BPLName",    T00."U_NAME";

-- - Título: Relatorio de devolução CR- auditoria - (0306)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de devolução cr- auditoria - (0306).
WITH    cte AS (     SELECT        DISTINCT T2."ReconDate",        T0."CANCELED",        T0."DocEntry",        T0."DocNum",        T0."CardCode",        T11."CardName",        T0."Serial",        T10."BPLName",        T0."DocDate",        T0."DocTotal",        T1."ReconSum",        CASE WHEN T2."ReconType" = 4 THEN 'Gerado nota de devolucao' WHEN T2."ReconType" = 3 THEN 'Baixa CR' WHEN T2."ReconType" = 0 THEN 'Nota reconciliada' END AS "Status",        T2."ReconDate" AS "Data contábil de fechamento da nota fiscal",        T0."DocStatus",        CASE WHEN T0."DocStatus" = 'O'        AND T2."CreateDate" IS NOT NULL THEN 'SALDO PARCIAL UTILIZADO' WHEN T0."DocStatus" = 'C'        AND T2."CreateDate" IS NOT NULL THEN 'FECHADO' END AS "NOTA FOI RECONCILIADA",        T5."DocDate" AS "Data_da_baixa",        T0."DocDueDate",        T5."DocNum" AS "DocNumContasAPagar",        T2."ReconNum" AS "DocNumReconciliacao",        T2."UserSign" AS "CodUsuario",        CASE WHEN T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido" = 'N' THEN 'NÃO' ELSE 'SIM' END AS "U_SDCanhotoRecebido",        T12."U_NAME"      FROM        ORIN T0        LEFT JOIN ITR1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."SrcObjAbs"        AND T1."SrcObjTyp" = 14        AND T1."ReconNum" NOT IN (         SELECT            T00."ReconNum"          FROM            OITR T00          WHERE            (             T00."Canceled" = 'Y'              or T00."ReconType" = 7           )       )        LEFT JOIN OITR T2 ON T1."ReconNum" = T2."ReconNum"         AND (         T2."Canceled" = 'N'          OR T2."Canceled" IS NULL       )        LEFT JOIN "@DE_PARA_CR" T4 ON T4."Code" = T0."CardCode"        LEFT JOIN RCT2 T3 ON T3."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry"  AND ROUND(T3."SumApplied"+ T3."DcntSum",2) = ROUND(T1."ReconSum" ,2)       AND T3."DocNum" NOT IN (         SELECT            T00."DocEntry"          FROM            ORCT T00          WHERE            T00."Canceled" = 'Y'       )        AND T3."InvType" = 14        LEFT JOIN ORCT T5 ON T5."DocEntry" = T3."DocNum" AND T2."ReconDate" = T5."DocDate"       AND T5."Canceled" = 'N'        AND T2."ReconType" = 3        LEFT JOIN OCRD T6 ON T6."CardCode" = T0."CardCode"        LEFT JOIN OCTG T7 ON T6."GroupNum" = T7."GroupNum"        LEFT JOIN INV1 T8 ON T8."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry"        LEFT JOIN OITM T9 ON T9."ItemCode" = T8."ItemCode"        LEFT JOIN OBPL T10 ON T10."BPLId" = T0."BPLId"        LEFT JOIN OCRD T11 ON T11."CardCode" = T0."CardCode"        LEFT JOIN OUSR T12 ON T12."INTERNAL_K" = T2."UserSign"        LEFT JOIN INV1 T13 ON T13."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry"      WHERE        (         T0."CANCELED" IN ('N', 'Y')       )        AND T2."ReconDate" >= [%1]        AND T2."ReconDate" <= [%2]        AND T13."Usage" NOT in (53)     )  SELECT    DISTINCT T00."ReconDate",    T00."CANCELED",    T00."DocEntry",    T00."DocNum",    T00."CardCode",    T00."CardName",    T00."Serial",    T00."BPLName",    T00."DocDate",    T00."Status",    T00."DocTotal",    T00."ReconSum",    T00."Data contábil de fechamento da nota fiscal",    T00."DocStatus",    T00."NOTA FOI RECONCILIADA",    T00."Data_da_baixa",    T00."DocDueDate",    T00."DocNumContasAPagar",    T00."DocNumReconciliacao",    T00."CodUsuario",    T00."U_SDCanhotoRecebido",    T00."U_NAME"  FROM    cte T00  GROUP BY    T00."ReconDate",    T00."CANCELED",    T00."DocEntry",    T00."DocNum",    T00."CardCode",    T00."CardName",    T00."Serial",    T00."BPLName",    T00."DocDate",    T00."Status",    T00."DocTotal",    T00."ReconSum",    T00."Data contábil de fechamento da nota fiscal",    T00."DocStatus",    T00."NOTA FOI RECONCILIADA",    T00."Data_da_baixa",    T00."DocDueDate",    T00."DocNumContasAPagar",    T00."DocNumReconciliacao",    T00."CodUsuario",    T00."U_SDCanhotoRecebido",    T00."BPLName",    T00."U_NAME";

-- - Título: Relatorio de entradas das empresas Manoel-RJ Manoel-PE - (0252)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de entradas das empresas manoel-rj manoel-pe - (0252).
SELECT  T0."DocNum", T0."CardCode",  T1."CardName", T2."BPLName",  T0."Serial", T3."NfmName", T3."NfmDescrip",   case when T0."DocStatus" ='O' THEN 'ABERTO' ELSE 'FECHADO' END AS "Status doc",   T0."DocDate",  T0."DocDueDate",   T0."DocTotal", T0."Comments"   FROM OPCH T0   INNER JOIN OCRD T1 ON T0."CardCode" = T1."CardCode"  INNER JOIN OBPL T2 ON T0."BPLId" = T2."BPLId" LEFT JOIN ONFM T3 ON T0."Model" = T3."AbsEntry"  WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."BPLId" in (6,9) AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."CardCode" NOT IN (SELECT T0."Code" from "@PARC_INTERCOMPANY" T0);

-- - Título: Relatorio de estoque de itens com minimo e maximo - (0195)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de estoque de itens com minimo e maximo - (0195).
SELECT  T0."ItemCode",  T0."ItemName", T2."ItmsGrpNam", T1."WhsCode",   T1."OnHand",  T1."MinStock",  T1."MaxStock"   FROM OITM T0   INNER JOIN OITW T1 ON T0."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode"  INNER JOIN OITB T2 ON T0."ItmsGrpCod" = T2."ItmsGrpCod"  WHERE T1."WhsCode"  LIKE '%%008' AND T2."ItmsGrpNam" =  '[%2]'  ORDER BY T0."ItemName" ASC;

-- - Título: Relatorio de estoque de itens com minimo, maximo com indicadores - (0240)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de estoque de itens com minimo, maximo com indicadores - (0240).
WITH CTE AS (SELECT T0."ItemCode", T0."ItemName", T2."ItmsGrpNam",T0."InvntryUom" ,T1."WhsCode", T1."OnHand", T1."MinStock", T1."MaxStock", CASE WHEN T1."OnHand">=T1."MinStock" AND T1."OnHand"<=T1."MaxStock" THEN '3-OK' WHEN T1."OnHand"<T1."MinStock" THEN '1-BAIXO' WHEN T1."OnHand">T1."MaxStock"  THEN '2-ALTO' END AS "SITUAÇÃO DO ESTOQUE"  FROM OITM T0   INNER JOIN OITW T1 ON T0."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode"  LEFT JOIN OITB T2 ON T2."ItmsGrpCod" = T0."ItmsGrpCod" WHERE T1."MinStock" >0 AND LENGTH(T1."WhsCode")>3 AND T1."WhsCode" NOT LIKE '%008')  SELECT * FROM CTE T00 ORDER BY T00."SITUAÇÃO DO ESTOQUE";

-- - Título: Relatorio de estoque de itens com minimo, maximo com indicadores Oficina - (0245)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de estoque de itens com minimo, maximo com indicadores oficina - (0245).
WITH CTE AS (SELECT T0."ItemCode", T0."ItemName", T2."ItmsGrpNam",T0."InvntryUom" ,T1."WhsCode", T1."OnHand", T1."MinStock", T1."MaxStock", CASE WHEN T1."OnHand">=T1."MinStock" AND T1."OnHand"<=T1."MaxStock" THEN '3-OK' WHEN T1."OnHand"<T1."MinStock" THEN '1-BAIXO' WHEN T1."OnHand">T1."MaxStock"  THEN '2-ALTO' END AS "SITUAÇÃO DO ESTOQUE"  FROM OITM T0   INNER JOIN OITW T1 ON T0."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode"  LEFT JOIN OITB T2 ON T2."ItmsGrpCod" = T0."ItmsGrpCod" WHERE T1."MinStock" >0 AND T1."WhsCode" LIKE '%008'), CTE2 AS (SELECT T0."ItemCode", T0."ItemName", T2."ItmsGrpNam",T0."InvntryUom" ,T1."WhsCode", T1."OnHand", T1."MinStock", T1."MaxStock",'4-SEM MAX/MIN DEFINIDO' AS "SITUAÇÃO DO ESTOQUE"  FROM OITM T0   INNER JOIN OITW T1 ON T0."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode"  LEFT JOIN OITB T2 ON T2."ItmsGrpCod" = T0."ItmsGrpCod" WHERE (T1."MinStock" =0 OR T1."MaxStock" =0) AND T1."OnHand">0  AND T1."WhsCode" LIKE '%008')  SELECT T01."ItemCode", T00."ItemName", T00."ItmsGrpNam",T00."InvntryUom" ,T00."WhsCode", T00."OnHand",T00."MinStock", T00."MaxStock",T00."SITUAÇÃO DO ESTOQUE"    FROM CTE T00 LEFT JOIN OITM T01 ON T01."ItemCode" = T00."ItemCode"    UNION ALL  SELECT T01."ItemCode", T00."ItemName", T00."ItmsGrpNam",T00."InvntryUom" ,T00."WhsCode", T00."OnHand",T00."MinStock", T00."MaxStock",T00."SITUAÇÃO DO ESTOQUE"   FROM CTE2 T00 LEFT JOIN OITM T01 ON T01."ItemCode" = T00."ItemCode"  ORDER BY T00."SITUAÇÃO DO ESTOQUE";

-- - Título: Relatorio de estrutura de produtos acabados (apenas com matéria prima e recursos) - (0101)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de estrutura de produtos acabados (apenas com matéria prima e recursos) - (0101).
SELECT T0."Code" as "Codigo Produto acabado", T2."ItemName" as "Descrição produto acabado" ,T0."Qauntity", CASE WHEN T1."Type" = 4 THEN 'Item' WHEN T1."Type" = 290 THEN 'Recurso' ELSE 'NÃO ENCONTRADO' END AS "Tipo de componente", T1."Code", T1."ItemName",T4."ItmsGrpNam" AS "Grupo de itens",  T1."Quantity",CASE WHEN T1."Type" = 290 THEN  T5."UnitOfMsr" ELSE T3."InvntryUom" END AS "Unidade de medida"  FROM OITT T0  INNER JOIN ITT1 T1 ON T0."Code" = T1."Father"  LEFT JOIN OITM T2 ON T2."ItemCode" = T0."Code" LEFT JOIN OITM T3 ON T3."ItemCode" = T1."Code" LEFT JOIN OITB T4 ON  T3."ItmsGrpCod" = T4."ItmsGrpCod" LEFT JOIN ORSC T5 ON  T5."VisResCode" = T1."Code"  WHERE T4."ItmsGrpCod" IN (119,120,121,122,123,124,125,131,137) OR  T1."Type" = 290  ORDER BY T0."Code",T1."Type";

-- - Título: Relatorio de faturamento de itens de ligação - (0149)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de faturamento de itens de ligação - (0149).
with cte as (SELECT T0."ItemCode", T0."ItemName",T1."ItmsGrpNam",  T0."InvntryUom",   (SELECT  SUM(T01."Quantity"*T02."NumInSale")  FROM OINV T00  INNER JOIN INV1 T01 ON T00."DocEntry" = T01."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OITM T02 ON T02."ItemCode" = T01."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITM T03 ON T03."ValidComm" = T02."ValidComm"   WHERE T00."CANCELED" = 'N' AND T01."Usage" in (15) and T03."ItemCode" = T0."ItemCode" and T02."ItmsGrpCod" in (119,122) AND T00."BPLId"  in (3,4,6,10)  AND T00."DocDate">=[%2] AND T00."DocDate"<=[%3] AND T00."U_NotaAjusteInterno" = 'N'  ) AS "Quantidade vendida", (SELECT  SUM(T01."LineTotal")  FROM OINV T00  INNER JOIN INV1 T01 ON T00."DocEntry" = T01."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OITM T02 ON T02."ItemCode" = T01."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITM T03 ON T03."ValidComm" = T02."ValidComm"   WHERE T00."CANCELED" = 'N' AND T01."Usage" in (15) and T03."ItemCode" = T0."ItemCode" and T02."ItmsGrpCod" in (119,122) AND T00."BPLId"  in (3,4,6,10)  AND T00."DocDate">=[%2] AND T00."DocDate"<=[%3] AND T00."U_NotaAjusteInterno" = 'N'  ) AS "Total R$ Faturado bruto"     FROM OITM T0  INNER JOIN OITB T1 ON T0."ItmsGrpCod" = T1."ItmsGrpCod"    WHERE T0."ItemCode" LIKE 'IL%'  AND T0."ItemCode" in ('IL0004','IL0009','IL0010','IL0012','IL0032','IL0039','IL0130','IL0127','IL0129','IL0178','IL0130','IL0136','IL0141')   GROUP BY T0."ItemCode", T0."ItemName",T1."ItmsGrpNam",  T0."InvntryUom",T0."NumInBuy"  ORDER BY T0."ItemName"), cte2 as (select *,  (SELECT  SUM(T01."LineTotal" )  FROM OINV T00  INNER JOIN INV1 T01 ON T00."DocEntry" = T01."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OITM T02 ON T02."ItemCode" = T01."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITM T03 ON T03."ValidComm" = T02."ValidComm"   WHERE T00."CANCELED" = 'N' AND T01."Usage" in (15) and T03."ItemCode" = T0."ItemCode" and T02."ItmsGrpCod" in (119,122) AND T00."BPLId"  in (3,4,6,10)  AND T00."DocDate">=[%2] AND T00."DocDate"<=[%3] AND T00."U_NotaAjusteInterno" = 'N'  )/T0."Quantidade vendida" AS "Preço venda médio R$"   from cte T0  order by t0."ItemName")   select * from cte2 T0;

-- - Título: Relatorio de faturamento de itens de ligação - (0149)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de faturamento de itens de ligação - (0149).
with cte as (SELECT T0."ItemCode", T0."ItemName",T1."ItmsGrpNam",  T0."InvntryUom",   (SELECT  SUM(T01."Quantity"*T02."NumInSale")  FROM OINV T00  INNER JOIN INV1 T01 ON T00."DocEntry" = T01."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OITM T02 ON T02."ItemCode" = T01."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITM T03 ON T03."ValidComm" = T02."ValidComm"   WHERE T00."CANCELED" = 'N' AND T01."Usage" in (15) and T03."ItemCode" = T0."ItemCode" and T02."ItmsGrpCod" in (119,122) AND T00."BPLId"  in (3,4,6,10)  AND T00."DocDate">=[%2] AND T00."DocDate"<=[%3] AND T00."U_NotaAjusteInterno" = 'N'  ) AS "Quantidade vendida", (SELECT  SUM(T01."LineTotal")  FROM OINV T00  INNER JOIN INV1 T01 ON T00."DocEntry" = T01."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OITM T02 ON T02."ItemCode" = T01."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITM T03 ON T03."ValidComm" = T02."ValidComm"   WHERE T00."CANCELED" = 'N' AND T01."Usage" in (15) and T03."ItemCode" = T0."ItemCode" and T02."ItmsGrpCod" in (119,122) AND T00."BPLId"  in (3,4,6,10)  AND T00."DocDate">=[%2] AND T00."DocDate"<=[%3] AND T00."U_NotaAjusteInterno" = 'N'  ) AS "Total R$ Faturado bruto"     FROM OITM T0  INNER JOIN OITB T1 ON T0."ItmsGrpCod" = T1."ItmsGrpCod"    WHERE T0."ItemCode" LIKE 'IL%'  AND T0."ItemCode" in ('IL0004','IL0009','IL0010','IL0012','IL0032','IL0039','IL0130','IL0127','IL0129','IL0178','IL0130','IL0136','IL0141')   GROUP BY T0."ItemCode", T0."ItemName",T1."ItmsGrpNam",  T0."InvntryUom",T0."NumInBuy"  ORDER BY T0."ItemName"), cte2 as (select *,  (SELECT  SUM(T01."LineTotal" )  FROM OINV T00  INNER JOIN INV1 T01 ON T00."DocEntry" = T01."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OITM T02 ON T02."ItemCode" = T01."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITM T03 ON T03."ValidComm" = T02."ValidComm"   WHERE T00."CANCELED" = 'N' AND T01."Usage" in (15) and T03."ItemCode" = T0."ItemCode" and T02."ItmsGrpCod" in (119,122) AND T00."BPLId"  in (3,4,6,10)  AND T00."DocDate">=[%2] AND T00."DocDate"<=[%3] AND T00."U_NotaAjusteInterno" = 'N'  )/T0."Quantidade vendida" AS "Preço venda médio R$"   from cte T0  order by t0."ItemName")   select * from cte2 T0;

-- - Título: Relatorio de faturamento de notas fiscais por itens (Recife) - (0183)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de faturamento de notas fiscais por itens (recife) - (0183).
SELECT T0."DocDate",T0."CardCode", T0."CardName", T1."ItemCode", T3."ItemName", T1."Quantity", T1."PriceBefDi", T0."Serial" as "Nro da nota fiscal", T2."BPLName" FROM OINV T0  INNER JOIN INV1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" INNER JOIN OBPL T2 ON T0."BPLId" = T2."BPLId" LEFT JOIN OITM T3 ON T3."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode" WHERE T1."Usage" in (15) AND T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."U_NotaAjusteInterno" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."BPLId" in (1,9) ORDER BY T0."DocDate",T0."CardCode",T3."ItemName";

-- - Título: Relatorio de faturamento por cl - (0225)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de faturamento por cl - (0225).
SELECT  T1."ItemCode", T2."ItemName", T2."SalUnitMsr", T3."ItmsGrpNam",  SUM(T1."Quantity") AS "Quantidade", SUM (T1."LineTotal") as "Valor R$",  SUM (T1."LineTotal")/ SUM(T1."Quantity")  AS "Preço médio R$ Unid. Medida de venda."   FROM OINV T0   INNER JOIN INV1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode"  INNER JOIN OITB T3 ON T2."ItmsGrpCod" = T3."ItmsGrpCod"  WHERE T0."BPLId" in (3,4,6,10) AND T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."U_NotaAjusteInterno" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T1."Usage" in (15) AND T3."ItmsGrpCod" IN (120,121)  and T0."CardCode" = [%3]  GROUP BY T1."ItemCode", T2."ItemName",T2."SalUnitMsr",T3."ItmsGrpNam" ORDER BY T3."ItmsGrpNam", T2."ItemName"  --POSSUI UMA PARTE DE INTERCOMPANY. NOTAS DE AJUSTE SÃO REMOVIDAS;

-- - Título: Relatorio de fluxos de contras-notas - (0292)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de fluxos de contras-notas - (0292).
SELECT  T12."TaxDate",  T12."DocDate", T0."DocNum",  T12."Serial" as "Nro NF", T4."Usage",  T3."ItemCode",  T3."ItemName",  T5."ItmsGrpNam", CASE WHEN T0."DocStatus" ='O' THEN 'ABERTO' ELSE 'FECHADO' END AS "Status" , T1."Quantity" as "Quantidade Pedido",  T11."Quantity" as "Quantidade NF" ,  CASE WHEN T1."Quantity">T11."Quantity" THEN 'Quantidade do Pedido MAIOR' WHEN T1."Quantity"<T11."Quantity" THEN 'Quantidade da NF MAIOR' ELSE 'OK' END AS "Analise_quantidade", T13."Quantity" AS "Quantidade NF Devolução" ,   T6."CardCode",  T6."CardName",  T7."BPLName", T1."PriceBefDi" as "Preço Pedido", T11."PriceBefDi" as "Preço NF", CASE WHEN T1."PriceBefDi">T11."PriceBefDi" THEN 'Preço do Pedido MAIOR' WHEN T1."Quantity"<T11."Quantity" THEN 'Preço da NF MAIOR' ELSE 'OK' END AS  "Analise_preco", T13."PriceBefDi" as "Preço NF devolucao"  FROM OPOR T0   INNER JOIN POR1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OITM T3 ON T1."ItemCode" = T3."ItemCode"  LEFT JOIN OUSG T4 ON T1."Usage" = T4."ID"  LEFT JOIN OITB T5 ON T3."ItmsGrpCod" = T5."ItmsGrpCod"  LEFT JOIN OCRD T6 ON T0."CardCode" = T6."CardCode"  LEFT JOIN OBPL T7 ON T0."BPLId" = T7."BPLId"  LEFT JOIN OSLP T8 ON T0."SlpCode" = T8."SlpCode" LEFT JOIN PDN1 T9 ON TO_VARCHAR(T9."BaseRef") = TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum") and TO_VARCHAR(T9."BaseLine") = TO_VARCHAR(T1."LineNum") LEFT JOIN OPDN T10 ON T10."DocEntry"  = T9."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN PCH1 T11 ON TO_VARCHAR(T11."BaseRef")  = TO_VARCHAR(T10."DocNum")  AND T11."BaseLine"  = T9."LineNum" AND T11."BaseType" = 20 LEFT JOIN OPCH T12 ON T12."DocEntry" = T11."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN RPC1 T13 ON TO_VARCHAR(T13."BaseRef") =TO_VARCHAR(T12."DocNum") AND T13."BaseLine" = T11."LineNum"  LEFT JOIN ORPC T14 ON T14."DocEntry" = T13."DocEntry"   WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T12."DocDate">=[%1]  AND T12."DocDate"<=[%2]   AND (T10."CANCELED" ='N' OR T10."CANCELED" IS NULL) AND   (T12."CANCELED" ='N' OR T12."CANCELED" IS NULL) AND  (T14."CANCELED" ='N' OR T14."CANCELED" IS NULL) AND T12."SeqCode" NOT IN (42,1,-2,38,39,-1) order by T6."CardCode", T0."DocNum", T3."ItemName";

-- - Título: Relatorio de fornecedores e emais - (0212)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de fornecedores e emais - (0212).
SELECT distinct T2."CardCode", T2."CardName", T2."E_Mail" FROM OPCH T0  INNER JOIN PCH1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" INNER JOIN OCRD T2 ON T0."CardCode" = T2."CardCode" WHERE T1."Usage" in (19,47)  AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."U_NotaAjusteInterno" ='N' AND T0."BPLId" in (1,9) order by  T2."CardName";

-- - Título: Relatorio de identificação de Pedido de compra MarketPlace Baseado Nota fiscal de entrada - (0107)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de identificação de pedido de compra marketplace baseado nota fiscal de entrada - (0107).
SELECT DISTINCT T0."DocNum" as "Nro Doc nota de entrada", T0."CardCode", T0."CardName", T0."DocDate", T0."DocDueDate", T0."TaxDate",T0."BPLName",T0."DocTotal",T0."Serial", case when T0."DocStatus" = 'C' THEN 'FECHADO' ELSE 'ABERTO' END AS "Status do doc", T3."CardCode" as "Parceiro do recebimento", T3."CardName", T4."BaseRef" as "Nro do pedido de compra"  FROM OPCH T0  LEFT JOIN PCH1 T1 ON T1."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OPDN T3 ON (TO_VARCHAR(T1."BaseRef") = TO_VARCHAR(T3."DocNum") ) AND (T1."BaseType" =20) LEFT JOIN PDN1 T4 ON T3."DocEntry" = T4."DocEntry" WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."BPLName" = [%3];

-- - Título: Relatorio de inadimplencia de notas de devolução - (0255)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de inadimplencia de notas de devolução - (0255).
SELECT T0."CardCode" AS "Codigo cliente",   T6."Name" as "Nome de para",    T0."CardName" AS "Razão Social",   T1."AliasName" AS "Nome fantasia",   T0."Serial" AS "Numero da nota fiscal",   T0."DocDate" AS "Data de lançamento",   T0."DocDueDate" AS "Data de vencimento",   T0."DocTotal" AS "Total da nota R$",   T0."DocTotal"-T0."PaidToDate" AS "Em aberto R$", -- Adicione esta linha   case when T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido" = 'Y' THEN 'SIM' ELSE 'NÃO' END AS "Canhoto Recebido",   T0."U_SDDataCanhoto",   T0."BPLName" AS "Filial",    S3."SlpName" AS "Nome do Vendedor",   T7."AgentName" AS "Nome gerente",   CRD1."State" AS "Estado",   T6."U_TipoDePagamento",   T6."U_Situacao" FROM ORIN T0 INNER JOIN OCRD T1 ON T0."CardCode" = T1."CardCode" LEFT JOIN OCTG T2 ON T0."GroupNum" = T2."GroupNum" LEFT JOIN OSLP S3 ON T1."SlpCode" = S3."SlpCode" LEFT JOIN CRD1 ON T0."CardCode" = CRD1."CardCode" AND CRD1."AdresType" = 'B' LEFT JOIN "@DE_PARA_CR" T6 ON T6."Code" = T0."CardCode"  LEFT JOIN OAGP T7 ON T7."AgentCode" = T1."AgentCode"  LEFT JOIN OBPL T8 ON T8."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE   T0."DocDueDate" >= [%0]   AND T0."DocDueDate" <= [%1]   AND T0."DocStatus" = 'O'   AND T0."CANCELED" IN ('N')    AND (   (T8."BPLName" IN ('NATURAL FARMS', 'RJ_FILIAL_NATURAL FARMS') AND '[%3]' IN ('NATURAL FARMS', 'RJ_FILIAL_NATURAL FARMS'))   OR    (T8."BPLName" IN ('SP_FILIAL_JFC &NATURAL SALADS', 'JFC &NATURAL SALADS') AND '[%3]' IN ('SP_FILIAL_JFC &NATURAL SALADS', 'JFC &NATURAL SALADS'))   OR    ( '[%3]' ='') )    ORDER BY T0."DocDueDate";

-- - Título: Relatorio de inadiplência consolidado - (0204)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de inadiplência consolidado - (0204).
SELECT  TRIM(T5."Name") AS "Nome CR", SUM(T0."DocTotal") -  SUM(T0."PaidSum") as "Valor total em aberto R$", TO_VARCHAR(T5."U_TipoDePagamento") as "Tipo", TO_VARCHAR(T5."U_Situacao") as "Situação do cliente"  FROM OINV T0 INNER JOIN OCRD T1 ON T0."CardCode" = T1."CardCode" LEFT JOIN OCTG T2 ON T0."GroupNum" = T2."GroupNum" LEFT JOIN OSLP S3 ON T0."SlpCode" = S3."SlpCode" LEFT JOIN CRD1 ON T0."CardCode" = CRD1."CardCode" AND CRD1."AdresType" = 'B' LEFT JOIN "@DE_PARA_CR" T5 ON T5."Code" = T0."CardCode"  LEFT JOIN OBPL T6 ON T6."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE   T0."DocDueDate" >= [%0]   AND T0."DocDueDate" <= [%1]   AND T0."DocStatus" = 'O'   AND T0."CANCELED" IN ('N')   AND T0."CardCode" NOT IN ('CL001471', 'CL001482', 'CL001520', 'CL002158', 'CL003964', 'CL001264', 'CL004824','CL005706') AND (   (T6."BPLName" IN ('NATURAL FARMS', 'RJ_FILIAL_NATURAL FARMS') AND '[%3]' IN ('NATURAL FARMS', 'RJ_FILIAL_NATURAL FARMS'))   OR    (T6."BPLName" IN ('SP_FILIAL_JFC &NATURAL SALADS', 'JFC &NATURAL SALADS') AND '[%3]' IN ('SP_FILIAL_JFC &NATURAL SALADS', 'JFC &NATURAL SALADS'))   OR    (T6."BPLName" = '[%3]') ) group by TRIM(T5."Name"),TO_VARCHAR(T5."U_TipoDePagamento"),TO_VARCHAR(T5."U_Situacao") order by SUM(T0."DocTotal")  desc;

-- - Título: Relatorio de itens cadastro - (0120)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de itens cadastro - (0120).
SELECT T0."ItemCode",T0."ItemName",T5."ItmsGrpNam",T0."FrgnName",T0."UpdateDate", T0."UserSign2", T4."U_NAME"  FROM OITM T0  LEFT JOIN OUSR T4 ON T0."UserSign2" = T4."USERID" LEFT JOIN OITB T5 ON T0."ItmsGrpCod" = T5."ItmsGrpCod" WHERE T0."validFor" = 'Y';

-- - Título: Relatorio de itens de ligação Compras - (0242)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de itens de ligação compras - (0242).
SELECT T0."ItemCode", T0."ItemName",T1."ItmsGrpNam",T0."NumInBuy", T0."BuyUnitMsr", T0."NumInSale",  T0."SalUnitMsr", T0."InvntryUom",  T2."ItemCode" as "Cod. Item Ligação", T2."ItemName" as "Nome item ligação" , T2."ItmsGrpCod",T3."ItmsGrpNam"  FROM OITM T0  INNER JOIN OITB T1 ON T0."ItmsGrpCod" = T1."ItmsGrpCod" LEFT JOIN OITM T2 ON  T2."ItemCode" = T0."ValidComm"  LEFT JOIN OITB T3 ON T3."ItmsGrpCod" = T2."ItmsGrpCod" WHERE T2."ItmsGrpCod"  IN (119,122) and T0."ValidComm" LIKE 'IL%%' AND T0."ItemCode" NOT LIKE 'IL%%' ORDER BY T0."ItemName" asc;

-- - Título: Relatorio de itens de ligação IL - (0069)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de itens de ligação il - (0069).
SELECT T0."ItemCode", T0."ItemName", T1."ItmsGrpCod", T1."ItmsGrpNam", T0."InvntryUom"  FROM OITM T0  INNER JOIN OITB T1 ON T0."ItmsGrpCod" = T1."ItmsGrpCod" WHERE T0."ItemCode" LIKE '%%IL%%' ORDER BY T0."ItemName";

-- - Título: Relatorio de itens faturados com preço médio Teresópolis - (0117)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de itens faturados com preço médio teresópolis - (0117).
SELECT T1."ItemCode", T4."ItemName", SUM(T1."Quantity") as "Quantidade faturada", SUM(T1."LineTotal") as "Valor Faturado R$",SUM(T1."LineTotal")/SUM(T1."Quantity") as "Preço médio R$",T0."CardCode", T2."CardName", T3."Name" AS "Nome da rede"  FROM OINV T0  INNER JOIN INV1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OCRD T2 ON T2."CardCode" = T0."CardCode"  LEFT JOIN "@SD_CADREDE" T3 ON T2."U_SD_Rede"  = T3."Code" LEFT JOIN OITM T4 ON T4."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode"   WHERE T0."CANCELED"  ='N' AND T1."Usage" = 15 AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."BPLId" in (3,4,6,10) AND T0."CardCode" NOT IN ('CL001471','CL001482','CL001520','CL002158','CL003964','CL001264')   GROUP BY T0."CardCode", T1."ItemCode", T4."ItemName",T2."CardName", T3."Name"  ORDER BY T3."Name",T1."ItemCode";

-- - Título: Relatorio de itens nota fiscal de entrada, com utilização e modelo de nota fiscal - (0115)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de itens nota fiscal de entrada, com utilização e modelo de nota fiscal - (0115).
SELECT T0."DocDate", T0."DocDueDate", T0."CardCode", T0."CardName", T0."DocNum",T0."Serial",T1."ItemCode", T1."Dscription", T1."Quantity", T1."PriceBefDi", T1."LineTotal",T2."Usage", T0."Comments",T4."NfmName", case when T0."DocStatus" = 'O' THEN 'Aberto' else 'Fechado' end as "Status do documento", T0."BPLName" FROM OPCH T0  INNER JOIN PCH1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" INNER JOIN OUSG T2 ON T1."Usage" = T2."ID" INNER JOIN ONFM T4 ON T0."Model" = T4."AbsEntry" LEFT JOIN OBPL T5 ON T5."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2]  AND T5."BPLName" = [%3];

-- - Título: Relatorio de itens sem item de ligação - (0244)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de itens sem item de ligação - (0244).
SELECT T0."ItemCode",  T0."ItemName", T1."ItmsGrpNam", T0."NumInBuy", T0."BuyUnitMsr", T0."NumInSale",  T0."SalUnitMsr", T0."InvntryUom",  T2."ItemCode" as "Cod. Item Ligação", T2."ItemName" as "Nome item ligação" , T2."ItmsGrpCod",T3."ItmsGrpNam"  FROM OITM T0   left JOIN OITB T1 ON T0."ItmsGrpCod" = T1."ItmsGrpCod" LEFT JOIN OITM T2 ON  T2."ItemCode" = T0."ValidComm"  LEFT JOIN OITB T3 ON T3."ItmsGrpCod" = T2."ItmsGrpCod" WHERE T1."ItmsGrpCod"  IN (119,122)  AND T0."ValidComm" IS NULL AND T0."ItemCode"  in (SELECT T02."ItemCode" FROM OPDN T00 INNER JOIN PDN1 T02 ON T02."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry" WHERE T00."CANCELED" ='N' AND T00."TaxDate">=[%1] AND T00."TaxDate"<=[%2] AND T00."CANCELED" ='N' AND T00."BPLId" in (3,4,6,10) AND T02."Usage" in (19,47) )   ORDER BY T0."ItemName" asc;

-- - Título: Relatorio de itens utilizados na entrada e na saída com totalizadores - (0044)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de itens utilizados na entrada e na saída com totalizadores - (0044).
SELECT DISTINCT T2."ItemCode", T1."Dscription",T3."ItmsGrpCod",  T3."ItmsGrpNam",'Item de compra' as "Onde é utilizado", COUNT(T1."ItemCode") AS "Quantidade de aparições", SUM(T1."LineTotal") as "TOTAL R$", MAX(T0."DocDate") as "Último uso", 'Pedido de compra' as "Tipo de documento", T4."BPLName" FROM OPOR T0  INNER JOIN POR1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" INNER JOIN OITB T3 ON T2."ItmsGrpCod" = T3."ItmsGrpCod" LEFT JOIN OBPL T4 ON T4."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate" >=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2]  GROUP BY  T2."ItemCode", T1."Dscription",T3."ItmsGrpCod",  T3."ItmsGrpNam",T4."BPLName"   UNION ALL   SELECT DISTINCT  T2."ItemCode", T1."Dscription",T3."ItmsGrpCod",  T3."ItmsGrpNam", 'Item de venda' as "Onde é utilizado",COUNT(T1."ItemCode") AS "Quantidade de aparições", SUM(T1."LineTotal") as "TOTAL R$", MAX(T0."DocDate") as "Último uso",  'Nota fiscal de saída' as "Tipo de documento",T4."BPLName"   FROM OINV T0  INNER JOIN INV1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" INNER JOIN OITB T3 ON T2."ItmsGrpCod" = T3."ItmsGrpCod" LEFT JOIN OBPL T4 ON T4."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate" >=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2]  GROUP BY  T2."ItemCode", T1."Dscription",T3."ItmsGrpCod",  T3."ItmsGrpNam",T4."BPLName"    ORDER BY  "TOTAL R$" DESC;

-- - Título: Relatorio de itens utilizados na entrada, saida detalhado - (0048)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de itens utilizados na entrada, saida detalhado - (0048).
SELECT DISTINCT T2."ItemCode", T1."Dscription",T3."ItmsGrpCod",  T3."ItmsGrpNam",'Item de compra' as "Onde é utilizado", COUNT(T1."ItemCode") AS "Quantidade de aparições", SUM(T1."LineTotal") as "TOTAL R$", MAX(T0."DocDate") as "Último uso", 'Pedido de compra' as "Tipo de documento", T4."BPLName", T2."BuyUnitMsr", T2."NumInBuy", T2."SalUnitMsr", T2."NumInSale",T2."InvntryUom" FROM OPOR T0  INNER JOIN POR1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" INNER JOIN OITB T3 ON T2."ItmsGrpCod" = T3."ItmsGrpCod" LEFT JOIN OBPL T4 ON T4."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate" >=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2]  GROUP BY  T2."ItemCode", T1."Dscription",T3."ItmsGrpCod",  T3."ItmsGrpNam",T4."BPLName", T2."BuyUnitMsr", T2."NumInBuy", T2."SalUnitMsr", T2."NumInSale",T2."InvntryUom"    UNION ALL   SELECT DISTINCT  T2."ItemCode", T1."Dscription",T3."ItmsGrpCod",  T3."ItmsGrpNam", 'Item de venda' as "Onde é utilizado",COUNT(T1."ItemCode") AS "Quantidade de aparições", SUM(T1."LineTotal") as "TOTAL R$", MAX(T0."DocDate") as "Último uso",  'Nota fiscal de saída' as "Tipo de documento", T4."BPLName", T2."BuyUnitMsr",T2."NumInBuy", T2."SalUnitMsr",T2."NumInSale",T2."InvntryUom"  FROM OINV T0  INNER JOIN INV1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" INNER JOIN OITB T3 ON T2."ItmsGrpCod" = T3."ItmsGrpCod" LEFT JOIN OBPL T4 ON T4."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate" >=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2]  GROUP BY  T2."ItemCode", T1."Dscription",T3."ItmsGrpCod",  T3."ItmsGrpNam",T4."BPLName", T2."BuyUnitMsr", T2."NumInBuy", T2."SalUnitMsr", T2."NumInSale",T2."InvntryUom"     ORDER BY  "TOTAL R$" DESC;

-- - Título: Relatorio de lancamentos LCM fornecedores nacionais - (0251)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de lancamentos lcm fornecedores nacionais - (0251).
SELECT T0."TransId", T0."TransType", T0."BaseRef", T0."RefDate", T1."Account", T1."Debit", T1."Credit", T1."ShortName", T02."U_NAME", T03."BPLName",T0."Memo"  FROM OJDT T0  INNER JOIN JDT1 T1 ON T0."TransId" = T1."TransId"  LEFT JOIN OUSR T02 ON to_varchar(T02."INTERNAL_K") = TO_VARCHAR(T0."UserSign") LEFT JOIN OBPL T03 ON T03."BPLId" = T1."BPLId" WHERE T1."Account"  ='2.01.01.01.01' and  T0."TransType" =30 AND T0."TransId" NOT IN (SELECT T0."StornoToTr"  FROM OJDT T0 WHERE T0."StornoToTr" IS NOT NULL)  AND T0."StornoToTr" IS NULL AND T0."RefDate">=[%1] AND T0."RefDate"<=[%2] ORDER BY T03."BPLName" DESC;

-- - Título: Relatorio de layouts de importação - (0309)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de layouts de importação - (0309).
SELECT T0."Code", T0."Name",T1."U_CardCode", T1."U_CNPJ_CPF" FROM "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@SD_LAYOUT"  T0  LEFT JOIN "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@SD_LAYOUT_2"  T1 ON T1."Code" = T0."Code";

-- - Título: Relatorio de lcms e seus documentos - (0256)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de lcms e seus documentos - (0256).
SELECT distinct  CASE T0."TransType"     WHEN 13 THEN 'Nota de saída'     WHEN 1470000071 THEN 'Depreciação'     WHEN 18 THEN 'Nota de entrada'     WHEN 20 THEN 'Recebimento'     WHEN 24 THEN 'Contas a receber'     WHEN 30 THEN 'LCM'     WHEN 46 THEN 'Contas a pagar'     WHEN 60 THEN 'Baixas de estoque'     ELSE 'Outros' END AS "Tipo de Transação", T0."BaseRef" as "Nro do doc" ,  T0."BPLName", CASE T0."TransType"     WHEN 13 THEN (select t00."DocTotal" FROM OINV T00 WHERE T00."DocNum" = T0."BaseRef")      WHEN 1470000071 THEN NULL     WHEN 18 THEN (select t00."DocTotal" FROM opch T00 WHERE T00."DocNum" = T0."BaseRef")      WHEN 20 THEN (select t00."DocTotal" FROM opdn T00 WHERE T00."DocNum" = T0."BaseRef")      WHEN 24 THEN (select t00."DocTotal" FROM ORCT T00 WHERE T00."DocNum" = T0."BaseRef")      WHEN 30 THEN (select t00."LocTotal" FROM OJDT T00 WHERE T00."BaseRef" = T0."BaseRef" and T00."TransType" = 30 )      WHEN 46 THEN (select t00."DocTotal" FROM OVPM T00 WHERE T00."DocNum" = T0."BaseRef"  )     WHEN 60 THEN (select t00."DocTotal" FROM OIGE T00 WHERE T00."DocNum" = T0."BaseRef" )       end as "Valor R$",        T0."TransId", T0."CreatedBy", T0."TaxDate", T0."UserSign", T1.User_code   FROM JDT1 T0  inner JOIN OUSR T1 ON T0."UserSign" = T1.USERID   WHERE T0."TransId" NOT IN (SELECT "TransId" from OJDT) ORDER BY T0."TaxDate" DESC;

-- - Título: Relatorio de lcms sems descrição - (0331)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de lcms sems descrição - (0331).
SELECT T0."BatchNum", T0."TransId", T0."BtfStatus", T0."BaseRef", T0."RefDate", T0."Memo", T0."TransType", T1."BPLName" FROM OJDT T0 INNER JOIN JDT1 T1 ON T0."TransId" = T1."TransId"  WHERE ( ( T0."Memo"  is NULL OR  T0."Memo" =''  ) AND (T1."LineMemo"  IS NULL OR T1."LineMemo" ='')   ) AND   T0."RefDate" >='2025-01-01' AND T0."RefDate"<='2025-12-31';

-- - Título: Relatorio de lista de preços - (0203)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de lista de preços - (0203).
SELECT T2."ListNum", T2."ListName",T0."ItemCode", T0."ItemName", T3."ItmsGrpNam", T1."Price" FROM OITM T0  INNER JOIN ITM1 T1 ON T0."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode" INNER JOIN OPLN T2 ON T1."PriceList" = T2."ListNum" INNER JOIN OITB T3 ON T0."ItmsGrpCod" = T3."ItmsGrpCod" WHERE T2."ValidFor" ='Y' AND  T1."Price" >0  AND T3."ItmsGrpCod"  IN (119,120,121,122,123,124,125,131) ORDER BY T2."ListName",T0."ItemName";

-- - Título: Relatorio de maiores captações no planilhão e seus faturamentos - (0259)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de maiores captações no planilhão e seus faturamentos - (0259).
WITH PLANILHAO_CANCELADOS AS (  SELECT T0."DocEntry" FROM "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@SD_PROC_SAIDA_MD"  T0 WHERE T0."Canceled"='Y'  ), CTE2 AS (  SELECT  T1."U_DateRef",  T1."U_CardCode", T1."U_ItemCode", T2."ItemName", T3."ItmsGrpNam", (SELECT MAX(T01."U_Quantity")  FROM "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@ASD_PROC_SAIDA_MD"  T00 LEFT JOIN "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@ASD_PROC_SAIDA"  T01  ON T01."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry" AND T01."LogInst" = T00."LogInst" WHERE T1."U_ItemCode" = T01."U_ItemCode" AND T1."U_CardCode" =T01."U_CardCode" and T1."U_DateRef" = T01."U_DateRef" AND T1."U_FilialEmpresa" =T01."U_FilialEmpresa" AND T0."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry") as "Maior quantidade captada" ,  --SUM(T1."U_Quantity") AS "Total_Quantity", (SELECT SUM(T01."Quantity")  FROM OINV T00  INNER JOIN INV1 T01 ON T01."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry"   WHERE T01."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode"  AND T00."CANCELED" ='N'  AND T1."U_CardCode"  = T00."CardCode" AND COALESCE(T00."U_TX_DtSaid",T00."DocDate")  =T1."U_DateRef" and T1."U_FilialEmpresa"=  T00."BPLId"  ) as "Quantidade faturada",  T1."U_PrecoUnit", (SELECT MAX(T01."U_Quantity")  FROM "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@ASD_PROC_SAIDA_MD"  T00 LEFT JOIN "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@ASD_PROC_SAIDA"  T01  ON T01."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry" AND T01."LogInst" = T00."LogInst" WHERE T1."U_ItemCode" = T01."U_ItemCode" AND T1."U_CardCode" =T01."U_CardCode" and T1."U_DateRef" = T01."U_DateRef" AND T1."U_FilialEmpresa" =T01."U_FilialEmpresa" AND T0."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry")  -(SELECT SUM(T01."Quantity")  FROM OINV T00  INNER JOIN INV1 T01 ON T01."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry"   WHERE T01."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode"  AND T00."CANCELED" ='N'  AND T1."U_CardCode"  = T00."CardCode" AND COALESCE(T00."U_TX_DtSaid",T00."DocDate")  =T1."U_DateRef" and T1."U_FilialEmpresa"=  T00."BPLId"  )  as "Quantidade cortada"    FROM "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@ASD_PROC_SAIDA_MD"  T0  LEFT JOIN "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@ASD_PROC_SAIDA"  T1  ON T1."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry" AND T1."LogInst" = T0."LogInst" LEFT JOIN OITM T2 ON T2."ItemCode" =T1."U_ItemCode"  LEFT JOIN OITB T3 ON T3."ItmsGrpCod" = T2."ItmsGrpCod" LEFT JOIN OITM T4 ON T4."ItemCode" =T2."ValidComm"   WHERE T0."Canceled" ='N' AND T1."U_DateRef" >= '2025-12-01' and T1."U_DateRef" <= '2025-12-31' AND   T2."ItmsGrpCod" IN (119,120,121,122,123,124,125,131,137)      AND T1."U_CardCode" NOT IN (         'CL002158', 'FO001424', 'CL001520', 'FO002947', 'CL001471',         'FO001340', 'FO000382', 'CL001482', 'FO001108', 'FO002087'     )     AND  LOCATE('-' || '1-9-5-8-3-4-6-10' || '-', '-' || TO_VARCHAR(T1."U_FilialEmpresa") || '-') > 0 AND T0."DocEntry" NOT IN ( SELECT * FROM PLANILHAO_CANCELADOS)   GROUP BY T2."NumInSale",T3."ItmsGrpCod", T3."ItmsGrpNam" ,T4."ItemName",T4."SalUnitMsr",    T1."U_PrecoUnit", T4."ItmsGrpCod",T1."U_DateRef", T1."U_ItemCode",T2."ItemName", IFNULL(NULLIF(T2."ValidComm", ''), T2."ItemCode"),T2."ItemCode",T1."U_CardCode",T1."U_FilialEmpresa", T0."DocEntry"   ORDER BY T2."ItemName")  SELECT *,T00."U_PrecoUnit" * T00."Quantidade cortada" AS "Valor cortado R$"  FROM CTE2 T00;

-- - Título: Relatorio de movimentação de itens compra e venda - (0318)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de movimentação de itens compra e venda - (0318).
SELECT T2."ItemCode", T2."ItemName", T3."ItmsGrpNam",T2."NumInBuy",T2."BuyUnitMsr",SUM(T1."Quantity"), SUM(T1."LineTotal") ,'COMPRA'  FROM OPCH T0   INNER JOIN PCH1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode"  INNER JOIN OITB T3 ON T2."ItmsGrpCod" = T3."ItmsGrpCod" WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T1."Usage" in (19,47) AND T0."U_NotaAjusteInterno" ='N' AND T0."BPLId" in (3,7) AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."CardCode" NOT IN (SELECT T00."Code" FROM "@PARC_INTERCOMPANY" T00)   GROUP BY  T2."ItemCode", T2."ItemName", T3."ItmsGrpNam",T2."NumInBuy",T2."BuyUnitMsr" UNION  ALL  SELECT T2."ItemCode", T2."ItemName", T3."ItmsGrpNam",T2."NumInSale",T2."SalUnitMsr",SUM(T1."Quantity"), SUM(T1."LineTotal") ,'VENDA'  FROM OINV T0   INNER JOIN INV1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode"  INNER JOIN OITB T3 ON T2."ItmsGrpCod" = T3."ItmsGrpCod"   WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T1."Usage" in (15,74) AND T0."U_NotaAjusteInterno" ='N' AND T0."BPLId" in (3,7) AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."CardCode" NOT IN (SELECT T00."Code" FROM "@PARC_INTERCOMPANY" T00)   GROUP BY T2."ItemCode", T2."ItemName", T3."ItmsGrpNam",T2."NumInSale",T2."SalUnitMsr";

-- - Título: Relatorio de movimentações contábeis por filiais - (0067)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de movimentações contábeis por filiais - (0067).
SELECT DISTINCT  T0."CardCode",T0."CardName",T0."CreateDate",T0."DocDate", T0."DocNum", T0."Serial", T0."DocTotal",T5."Usage",T3."AcctCode",  T3."AcctName" , T2."Debit", T2."Credit", 'NOTA DE SAÍDA' AS "Tipo de Nota" FROM OINV T0  INNER JOIN OJDT T1 ON T0."TransId" = T1."TransId" INNER JOIN JDT1 T2 ON T1."TransId" = T2."TransId" INNER JOIN OACT T3 ON T2."Account" = T3."AcctCode"  LEFT JOIN INV1 T4 ON T0."DocEntry" = T4."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OUSG T5 ON T4."Usage" = T5."ID"   WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] and T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."BPLName" = [%5] AND T0."CardCode" IN ('CL002158','CL003964')   UNION ALL  SELECT DISTINCT T0."CardCode",T0."CardName",T0."CreateDate",T0."DocDate",  T0."DocNum", T0."Serial", T0."DocTotal", T5."Usage",T3."AcctCode",  T3."AcctName" , T2."Debit", T2."Credit",'NOTA DE ENTRADA' AS "Tipo de Nota" FROM OPCH T0  INNER JOIN OJDT T1 ON T0."TransId" = T1."TransId" INNER JOIN JDT1 T2 ON T1."TransId" = T2."TransId"  INNER JOIN OACT T3 ON T2."Account" = T3."AcctCode" LEFT JOIN PCH1 T4 ON T0."DocEntry" = T4."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OUSG T5 ON T4."Usage" = T5."ID"  WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] and T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."BPLName" = [%5] AND T0."CardCode" IN ('FO001108','FO005273')  ORDER BY T0."DocNum";

-- - Título: Relatorio de movimentações de fatura fla - (0265)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de movimentações de fatura fla - (0265).
SELECT  T0."DocNum",  T0."DocDate",  T0."DocDueDate",  T0."CardCode",  T0."CardName",  T0."BPLName", T0."DocTotal" , (SELECT SUM(T00."DocTotal")  FROM ODPO T00 INNER JOIN DPO1 T01 ON T01."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry" WHERE T00."CANCELED" ='N' AND T01."BaseType"  = 22 AND TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum") = TO_VARCHAR(T01."BaseRef") AND   T00."DocNum" NOT IN (SELECT T001."BaseRef" FROM ORPC  T000 INNER JOIN RPC1 T001 ON T001."DocEntry" = T000."DocEntry" WHERE T000."CANCELED" ='N' AND T001."BaseType" = 204)  )  AS "Valor adiantado", (SELECT STRING_AGG(T00."DocNum",',')  FROM ODPO T00 INNER JOIN DPO1 T01 ON T01."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry" WHERE T00."CANCELED" ='N' AND T01."BaseType"  = 22 AND TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum") = TO_VARCHAR(T01."BaseRef")  AND   T00."DocNum" NOT IN (SELECT T001."BaseRef" FROM ORPC  T000 INNER JOIN RPC1 T001 ON T001."DocEntry" = T000."DocEntry" WHERE T000."CANCELED" ='N' AND T001."BaseType" = 204)  ) AS "Nro doc Faturas de adiantamento" , (SELECT STRING_AGG(TO_VARCHAR(T00."DocDate",'DD/MM/YYYY'),',')  FROM ODPO T00 INNER JOIN DPO1 T01 ON T01."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry" WHERE T00."CANCELED" ='N' AND T01."BaseType"  = 22 AND TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum") = TO_VARCHAR(T01."BaseRef")  AND   T00."DocNum" NOT IN (SELECT T001."BaseRef" FROM ORPC  T000 INNER JOIN RPC1 T001 ON T001."DocEntry" = T000."DocEntry" WHERE T000."CANCELED" ='N' AND T001."BaseType" = 204)  ) AS "Nro doc Faturas de adiantamento"    FROM OPOR T0 WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."CardCode" = 'FO004702';

-- - Título: Relatorio de movimentações de item de ligação - (0243)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de movimentações de item de ligação - (0243).
with cte as (SELECT T0."ItemCode", T0."ItemName",T1."ItmsGrpNam",  T0."InvntryUom",  (SELECT MIN(T00."TaxDate")   FROM OPDN T00  INNER JOIN PDN1 T01 ON T00."DocEntry" = T01."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OITM T02 ON T02."ItemCode" = T01."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITM T03 ON T03."ValidComm" = T02."ValidComm"   WHERE T00."CANCELED" = 'N' AND T01."Usage" in (19,47) and T03."ItemCode" = T0."ItemCode" and T02."ItmsGrpCod" in (119,122) AND T00."BPLId" in (3,4,6,10) AND T00."TaxDate">=[%2] AND T00."TaxDate"<=[%3] AND T00."U_NotaAjusteInterno" ='N' AND UPPER(T00."Comments") NOT LIKE '%%(PF)%%' ) AS "Data documento recebimento",   (SELECT MAX(COALESCE(T00."U_TX_DtSaid",T00."DocDate"))   FROM OINV T00  INNER JOIN INV1 T01 ON T00."DocEntry" = T01."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OITM T02 ON T02."ItemCode" = T01."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITM T03 ON T03."ValidComm" = T02."ValidComm"   WHERE T00."CANCELED" = 'N' AND T01."Usage" in (15) and T03."ItemCode" = T0."ItemCode" and T02."ItmsGrpCod" in (119,122) AND T00."BPLId"  in (3,4,6,10)  AND  COALESCE(T00."U_TX_DtSaid",T00."DocDate")>=add_days([%2],1) AND COALESCE(T00."U_TX_DtSaid",T00."DocDate")<=add_days([%3],1) AND T00."U_NotaAjusteInterno" ='N'  ) AS "Data de entrega de venda", (SELECT SUM(T01."Quantity")  FROM OPDN T00  INNER JOIN PDN1 T01 ON T00."DocEntry" = T01."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OITM T02 ON T02."ItemCode" = T01."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITM T03 ON T03."ValidComm" = T02."ValidComm"   WHERE T00."CANCELED" = 'N' AND T01."Usage" in (19,47) and T03."ItemCode" = T0."ItemCode" and T02."ItmsGrpCod" in (119,122) AND T00."BPLId" in (3,4,6,10) AND T00."TaxDate">=[%2] AND T00."TaxDate"<=[%3] AND T00."U_NotaAjusteInterno" ='N' AND UPPER(T00."Comments") NOT LIKE '%%(PF)%%' ) AS "Quantidade comprada original", (SELECT SUM(T01."Quantity" * T02."NumInBuy")  FROM OPDN T00  INNER JOIN PDN1 T01 ON T00."DocEntry" = T01."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OITM T02 ON T02."ItemCode" = T01."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITM T03 ON T03."ValidComm" = T02."ValidComm"   WHERE T00."CANCELED" = 'N' AND T01."Usage" in (19,47) and T03."ItemCode" = T0."ItemCode" and T02."ItmsGrpCod" in (119,122) AND T00."BPLId" in (3,4,6,10) AND T00."TaxDate">=[%2] AND T00."TaxDate"<=[%3] AND T00."U_NotaAjusteInterno" ='N' AND UPPER(T00."Comments") NOT LIKE '%%(PF)%%' ) AS "Quantidade comprada",   (SELECT SUM(T01."Quantity"*T02."NumInSale")  FROM OINV T00  INNER JOIN INV1 T01 ON T00."DocEntry" = T01."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OITM T02 ON T02."ItemCode" = T01."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITM T03 ON T03."ValidComm" = T02."ValidComm"   WHERE T00."CANCELED" = 'N' AND T01."Usage" in (15) and T03."ItemCode" = T0."ItemCode" and T02."ItmsGrpCod" in (119,122) AND T00."BPLId"  in (3,4,6,10)  AND  COALESCE(T00."U_TX_DtSaid",T00."DocDate")>=add_days([%2],1) AND COALESCE(T00."U_TX_DtSaid",T00."DocDate")<=add_days([%3],1) AND T00."U_NotaAjusteInterno" ='N'  ) AS "Quantidade vendida"   FROM OITM T0  INNER JOIN OITB T1 ON T0."ItmsGrpCod" = T1."ItmsGrpCod"    WHERE T0."ItemCode" LIKE 'IL%'  AND  T0."ItmsGrpCod" =119 GROUP BY T0."ItemCode", T0."ItemName",T1."ItmsGrpNam",  T0."InvntryUom",T0."NumInBuy"  ORDER BY T0."ItemName"), cte2 as (select *  from cte T0  order by t0."ItemName")   select * from cte2 T0 where (T0."Quantidade vendida"+ T0."Quantidade comprada")>0;

-- - Título: Relatorio de notas abertas MC_DONALDS-TERESOPOLIS - (0313)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de notas abertas mc_donalds-teresopolis - (0313).
SELECT DISTINCT  T2."BPLName",  T0."CardCode",  T0."CardName", T3."TaxId0" as "Cnpj", CASE WHEN T0."CardCode" ='CL000001' THEN 'Rod. BR-101 Sul, 5225 – Centro – Galpão 02, Cabo de Santo Agostinho – PE, CEP 54510-000, Brasil' WHEN T0."CardCode" ='CL000002' THEN 'Av. Paul Garfunkel, 300 – Cidade Industrial, Curitiba – PR, CEP 81460-040, Brasil' WHEN T0."CardCode" ='CL000582' THEN 'Rua Harold Barnsley Holland, 2130 – Rio Abaixo, Jacareí – SP, CEP 12334-403, Brasil' WHEN T0."CardCode" ='CL000581' THEN 'Av. das Comunicações, 333 – PQ Ind Anhanguera, Osasco – SP, CEP 06.276-190, Brasil' WHEN T0."CardCode" ='CL002545' THEN 'Av. Papa João Paulo I, 26 – Bonsucesso, Guarulhos – SP, CEP 07174-005, Brasil' ELSE 'SEM ENDEREÇO DEFINIDO'  END AS "Endereço" , T0."Serial", T0."DocDate", T0."DocDueDate",  T0."DocTotal", T0."PaidSum"   FROM OINV T0   INNER JOIN INV1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"   INNER JOIN OBPL T2 ON T0."BPLId" = T2."BPLId" LEFT JOIN INV12 T3 ON T3."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry"      WHERE T0."CardCode" IN ('CL000001','CL000002','CL000581','CL000582','CL002545') AND T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T1."Usage" in (15,74) and T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."DocStatus" ='O' AND T0."BPLId"  in (3,7);

-- - Título: Relatorio de notas assinadas - (0319)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de notas assinadas - (0319).
SELECT  T0."DocNum", T0."CardCode",  T0."CardName", T0."DocTotal", T0."DocDueDate", T0."TaxDate",  T1."Descript", T0."Serial",  T0."U_ProtocoloAssinatura",  T0."U_CompradorResponsavel"     FROM OPCH T0  LEFT JOIN OPYM  T1 ON T1."PayMethCod" = T0."PeyMethod" WHERE T0."U_ProtocoloAssinatura" is not null AND T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDueDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDueDate"<=[%2] ORDER BY T0."U_ProtocoloAssinatura",T0."CardName" ASC;

-- - Título: Relatorio de notas boleto SALADS sap - (0316)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de notas boleto salads sap - (0316).
SELECT distinct T3."BPLName", T0."CardCode", T0."CardName", T12."TaxId0",T0."Address",T0."Serial", T0."DocDate", T0."DocDueDate", T0."DocTotal",T0."PaidSum",T0."DocDueDate",T13."PymntGroup", CASE WHEN T0."DocStatus" ='O' THEN 'ABERTO' ELSE 'FECHADO' END AS "STATUS" FROM OINV T0   INNER JOIN INV1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OCRD T2 ON T0."CardCode" = T2."CardCode"  INNER JOIN OBPL T3 ON T0."BPLId" = T3."BPLId" LEFT JOIN INV12 T12 ON T0."DocEntry" = T12."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OCTG T13 ON T13."GroupNum" = T0."GroupNum"  WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2]  AND T1."Usage" in (15,74) AND T0."BPLId" in (3,7) AND  T2."U_PeriodicidadeDoBoleto" ='NotaBoleto';

-- - Título: Relatorio de notas boleto SALADS, sem confirmação no banco - (0314)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de notas boleto salads, sem confirmação no banco - (0314).
WITH CTE AS (SELECT DISTINCT  T0."DocEntry", T0."DocNum", T0."CardCode", T0."CardName",T0."Serial",T0."BPLName", T0."DocDate", T0."DocDueDate", CASE WHEN T3."Description" = 'Confirmado' and  DAYS_BETWEEN(T0."DocDueDate",current_date) >0 then  DAYS_BETWEEN(T0."DocDueDate",current_date)  end as "Dias vencido",T0."DocTotal",T5."Usage", CASE WHEN T4."U_Boleto" IS NOT NULL  THEN T4."U_Boleto" ELSE 'Não está marcado como boleto no PN' end as "Boleto", T0."DocStatus",     T4."U_PeriodicidadeDoBoleto",T2."OurNumber",T2."PayMethodCode", T2."DateCreate" as "Data de criação do boleto no SAP",T2."DocDate" as "Data contábil do boleto",T2."DueDate" as "Data de vencimento do boleto",T2."ValueDocument",T2."Document",T2."InstallmentID",T1."DicountValue",T1."InstallmentValue",T2."ValueInterestDaysOfLate", T3."Description", T2."DataDoPagamento",T7."Description" as "Situação", T6."Name", T9."InstDays" as "Prazo para pagamento",  T0."U_SDDataCanhoto" AS "Canhoto recebido",T2."DescontoFinanceiro", T0."PaidSum", T0."Address" FROM OINV T0 LEFT JOIN "IntegrationBank"."IV_IB_BillOfExchange" T2 ON T0."DocEntry" = T2."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN "IntegrationBank"."IV_IB_BillOfExchangeInstallment"  T1 ON T1."BoeId" = T2."ID"  LEFT JOIN "IntegrationBank"."IV_IB_BoeStatus" T3 ON T2."Status" = T3."ID" LEFT JOIN "IntegrationBank"."IV_IB_BillOfExchangeSituation" T7 ON T7."ID" = T2."Situation" LEFT JOIN OCRD T4 ON T4."CardCode"  = T0."CardCode"  LEFT JOIN "@SD_ROTA" T6 ON T4."U_SD_Rede" = T6."Code" INNER JOIN INV1 T5 ON T0."DocEntry" = T5."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OCTG T8 ON T0."GroupNum" = T8."GroupNum" LEFT JOIN  CTG1 T9 ON T8."GroupNum" = T9."CTGCode" WHERE (T0."DocDate" between [%1] and [%2]) and  (T4."U_Boleto" = 'Sim' OR T2."ValueDocument" >0) AND (T0."CANCELED" ='N') and (T5."Usage" IN ( 15,74)) and  ((T3."Description" not in ('Cancelado') OR T3."Description" is null))  AND T0."BPLName"  <> 'NATURAL FARMS' and T0."BPLId"  IN (3,7)  union all  SELECT DISTINCT  T0."DocEntry",T0."DocNum", T0."CardCode", T0."CardName",T0."Serial",T0."BPLName", T0."DocDate" as "Data de emissão da nota fiscal", T0."DocDueDate", CASE WHEN T3."Description" = 'Confirmado' and  DAYS_BETWEEN(T0."DocDueDate",current_date) >0 then  DAYS_BETWEEN(T0."DocDueDate",current_date)  end as "Dias vencido",T0."DocTotal",T5."Usage", CASE WHEN T4."U_Boleto" IS NOT NULL  THEN T4."U_Boleto" ELSE 'Não está marcado como boleto no PN' end as "Boleto", T0."DocStatus",    T4."U_PeriodicidadeDoBoleto",T2."OurNumber",T2."PayMethodCode", T2."DateCreate" as "Data de criação do boleto no SAP",T2."DocDate" as "Data contábil do boleto",T2."DueDate" as "Data de vencimento do boleto",T2."ValueDocument",T2."Document",T2."InstallmentID",T1."DicountValue",T1."InstallmentValue",T2."ValueInterestDaysOfLate", T3."Description", T2."DataDoPagamento",T7."Description" as "Situação", T6."Name", T9."InstDays" as "Prazo para pagamento",T0."U_SDDataCanhoto" AS "Canhoto recebido",T2."DescontoFinanceiro",T0."PaidSum", T0."Address" FROM OINV T0 INNER JOIN "IntegrationBank"."IV_IB_BillOfExchangeInstallment" T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN "IntegrationBank"."IV_IB_BillOfExchange"  T2 ON T1."BoeId" = T2."ID"  LEFT JOIN "IntegrationBank"."IV_IB_BoeStatus" T3 ON T2."Status" = T3."ID" LEFT JOIN "IntegrationBank"."IV_IB_BillOfExchangeSituation" T7 ON T7."ID" = T2."Situation" LEFT JOIN OCRD T4 ON T4."CardCode"  = T0."CardCode"  LEFT JOIN "@SD_ROTA" T6 ON T4."U_SD_Rede" = T6."Code" INNER JOIN INV1 T5 ON T0."DocEntry" = T5."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OCTG T8 ON T0."GroupNum" = T8."GroupNum" LEFT JOIN CTG1 T9 ON T8."GroupNum" = T9."CTGCode" WHERE (T0."DocDate" between [%1] and [%2]) and  (T4."U_Boleto" = 'Sim' OR T2."ValueDocument" >0) AND (T0."CANCELED" ='N') and (T5."Usage" IN ( 15,74) ) and  ((T3."Description" not in ('Cancelado') OR T3."Description" is null)) AND  T0."BPLName"  <> 'NATURAL FARMS'  and T0."BPLId"  IN (3,7) )  SELECT T0."BPLName",T0."CardCode",T0."CardName",T12."TaxId0",T0."Address",T0."Serial",T0."DocDate", T0."DocDueDate",T0."DocTotal", T0."PaidSum" FROM CTE T0 LEFT JOIN INV12 T12 ON T0."DocEntry" = T12."DocEntry"  WHERE T0."Description" in ('Gerado','',NULL) AND T0."Document" <> '' and T0."DescontoFinanceiro" = 0;

-- - Título: Relatorio de notas canceladas e seus canhotos - (0269)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de notas canceladas e seus canhotos - (0269).
WITH CTE AS (SELECT     T0."DocNum", T0."DocTotal",T2."BPLName",T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido", T0."CANCELED",T0."CANCELED",T1."BaseRef",T0."DocDate" FROM OINV T0 LEFT JOIN INV1 T1 ON T1."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OBPL T2 ON T2."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE T0."CANCELED" IN ('C') AND T0."DocDate">='2026-01-01'  AND  T0."BPLId"  not in (1,9)  AND T1."Usage"  in (15,74) ),FORA_DO_PRAZO AS  (  SELECT     T0."DocNum",T0."DocTotal",T2."BPLName",T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido",T0."CANCELED",'N',T1."BaseRef",T0."DocDate" FROM ORIN T0 LEFT JOIN RIN1 T1 ON T1."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OBPL T2 ON T2."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE T0."CANCELED" IN ('N') AND  T0."DocDate">='2026-01-01'   AND T0."BPLId"  not in (1,9) and T1."BaseRef" IS NOT NULL AND T1."Usage"  in (15,74) AND T1."BaseType" = 13 ), CONSOLIDADO AS ( SELECT T0."DocNum",T0."DocTotal",T2."BPLName",T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido", T0."CANCELED",'N' AS "FORA_DO_PRAZO",'Y'AS "CONSIDERADO_COMO_CANCELADO",(select DISTINCT TO_VARCHAR(T00."DocDate") FROM CTE T00 WHERE TO_VARCHAR(T00."BaseRef") = TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum"))  as "DATA_CANCELAMENTO" FROM OINV T0 LEFT JOIN OBPL T2 ON T2."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum") in (select TO_VARCHAR(T00."BaseRef") FROM CTE T00)  UNION ALL  SELECT T0."DocNum", T0."DocTotal",T2."BPLName",T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido", T0."CANCELED",'Y','Y',(select DISTINCT TO_VARCHAR(T00."DocDate") FROM FORA_DO_PRAZO  T00 WHERE TO_VARCHAR(T00."BaseRef") = TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum")) as "DATA_CANCELAMENTO" FROM OINV T0 LEFT JOIN OBPL T2 ON T2."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum") in (select TO_VARCHAR(T00."BaseRef") FROM FORA_DO_PRAZO  T00))   SELECT *, (SELECT T00."DocDate" FROM OINV T00 WHERE T00."DocNum" = T0."DocNum")  AS "DATA EMISSÃO"  ,(SELECT T00."Serial" FROM OINV T00 WHERE T00."DocNum" = T0."DocNum")  AS "Nro nota fiscal"    FROM CONSOLIDADO T0;

-- - Título: Relatorio de notas canceladas e seus canhotos- com data de lançamento - (0272)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de notas canceladas e seus canhotos- com data de lançamento - (0272).
WITH CTE AS ( SELECT      T0."DocNum",     T0."DocTotal",     T2."BPLName",     T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido",     T0."CANCELED",     T1."BaseRef",     T0."DocDate" FROM OINV T0 LEFT JOIN INV1 T1 ON T1."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OBPL T2 ON T2."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE      T0."CANCELED" = 'C'       AND T1."Usage" IN (15,74) ),  FORA_DO_PRAZO AS ( SELECT      T0."DocNum",     T0."DocTotal",     T2."BPLName",     T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido",     T0."CANCELED",     'N' AS "FLAG",     T1."BaseRef",     T0."DocDate" FROM ORIN T0 LEFT JOIN RIN1 T1 ON T1."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OBPL T2 ON T2."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE      T0."CANCELED" = 'N'     AND T1."BaseRef" IS NOT NULL     AND T1."Usage" IN (15,74)     AND T1."BaseType" = 13 ),  CONSOLIDADO AS (  SELECT      T0."DocNum",     T0."DocTotal",     T2."BPLName",     T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido",     T0."CANCELED",     'N' AS "FORA_DO_PRAZO",     'Y' AS "CONSIDERADO_COMO_CANCELADO",     (         SELECT MIN(T00."DocDate")         FROM CTE T00         WHERE TO_VARCHAR(T00."BaseRef") = TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum")     ) AS "DATA_CANCELAMENTO" FROM OINV T0 LEFT JOIN OBPL T2 ON T2."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum") IN (     SELECT TO_VARCHAR(T00."BaseRef") FROM CTE T00 )  UNION ALL  SELECT      T0."DocNum",     T0."DocTotal",     T2."BPLName",     T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido",     T0."CANCELED",     'Y',     'Y',     (         SELECT MIN(T00."DocDate")         FROM FORA_DO_PRAZO T00         WHERE TO_VARCHAR(T00."BaseRef") = TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum")     ) FROM OINV T0 LEFT JOIN OBPL T2 ON T2."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum") IN (     SELECT TO_VARCHAR(T00."BaseRef") FROM FORA_DO_PRAZO T00 ) ),  CTE2 AS (  SELECT      T0."DocNum" AS "Doc",     T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido",     T0."UpdateDate" FROM ADOC T0 WHERE      T0."DocNum" IN (SELECT "DocNum" FROM CONSOLIDADO)     AND T0."ObjType" = 13  UNION ALL  SELECT      T0."DocNum",     T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido",     T0."UpdateDate" FROM OINV T0 WHERE      T0."DocNum" IN (SELECT "DocNum" FROM CONSOLIDADO)  ),  NOTAS AS (  SELECT      T0."Doc",     MIN(T0."UpdateDate") AS "Data de entrada canhoto" FROM CTE2 T0 WHERE T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido" = 'Y' GROUP BY T0."Doc"  )  SELECT      T0.*,     T1."DocDate" AS "DATA EMISSÃO",     T1."Serial" AS "Nro nota fiscal",     T2."Data de entrada canhoto" FROM CONSOLIDADO T0 LEFT JOIN OINV T1 ON T1."DocNum" = T0."DocNum" LEFT JOIN NOTAS T2 ON T2."Doc" = T0."DocNum";

-- - Título: Relatorio de notas canceladas, cancelamentos fora do prazo e etc - (0118)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de notas canceladas, cancelamentos fora do prazo e etc - (0118).
SELECT DISTINCT T0."DocEntry", CASE WHEN T0."CANCELED" ='N' THEN 'NÃO CANCELADO' WHEN  T0."CANCELED" ='Y' THEN 'CANCELADO' END AS "Situação documento de marketing SAP",  T0."DocNum", T0."CardCode", T0."CardName", T0."BPLName", T3."SeqName", T0."Serial", T0."DocTotal", T0."DocTime", T0."DocDate", T2."U_NAME",TO_VARCHAR( T0. "Comments"),  case when  T0."DocStatus" = 'O' THEN 'ABERTO' ELSE 'FECHADO' END AS "Status documento",   TableChaveAcesso."KeyNfe" AS "Chave de Acesso",   Substring(TableChaveAcesso."KeyNfe", 27,8) AS "Nro nota Addon",   T7."Description",'NOTA DE SAÍDA' AS "Tipo de documento"  FROM OINV T0  INNER JOIN INV12 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN INV1 T5 ON T0."DocEntry" = T5."DocEntry" INNER JOIN OUSR T2 ON T0."UserSign2" = T2."USERID"  INNER JOIN NFN1 T3 ON T0."SeqCode"  = T3."SeqCode"  INNER JOIN OBPL T4 ON T4."BPLId" = T0."BPLId"  LEFT JOIN  "DBInvOne"."Process" TableChaveAcesso  ON T0."DocEntry"  = TableChaveAcesso."DocEntry" AND TableChaveAcesso."DocType" = 13 AND  Substring(TableChaveAcesso."KeyNfe", 27,8) = T0."Serial" AND  TableChaveAcesso."CompanyId" in (1,2,3,4,5,6,7,8,9) LEFT JOIN "DBInvOne"."ProcessStatus" T7 ON T7."ID" = TableChaveAcesso."StatusId" WHERE  T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."SeqCode" <> - 2 AND T0."CANCELED" IN ('Y','N')   UNION ALL  SELECT DISTINCT T0."DocEntry",CASE WHEN T0."CANCELED" ='N' THEN 'NÃO CANCELADO' WHEN  T0."CANCELED" ='Y' THEN 'CANCELADO' END AS "Situação documento de marketing SAP" ,T0."DocNum", T0."CardCode", T0."CardName", T0."BPLName", T3."SeqName", T0."Serial", T0."DocTotal", T0."DocTime", T0."DocDate", T2."U_NAME",TO_VARCHAR( T0. "Footer"),  case when  T0."DocStatus" = 'O' THEN 'ABERTO' ELSE 'FECHADO' END AS "Status documento",   TableChaveAcesso."KeyNfe" AS "Chave de Acesso",   Substring(TableChaveAcesso."KeyNfe", 27,8) AS "Nro nota Addon",   T7."Description", 'CANCELAMENTO FORA DO PRAZO' AS "Tipo de documento"  FROM ORIN T0  INNER JOIN RIN12 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN RIN1 T5 ON T0."DocEntry" = T5."DocEntry" INNER JOIN OUSR T2 ON T0."UserSign2" = T2."USERID"  INNER JOIN NFN1 T3 ON T0."SeqCode"  = T3."SeqCode"  INNER JOIN OBPL T4 ON T4."BPLId" = T0."BPLId"  LEFT JOIN  "DBInvOne"."Process" TableChaveAcesso  ON T0."DocEntry"  = TableChaveAcesso."DocEntry" AND TableChaveAcesso."DocType" = 14 AND  Substring(TableChaveAcesso."KeyNfe", 27,8) = T0."Serial" AND  TableChaveAcesso."CompanyId" in (1,2,3,4,5,6,7,8,9) LEFT JOIN "DBInvOne"."ProcessStatus" T7 ON T7."ID" = TableChaveAcesso."StatusId" WHERE  T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."SeqCode" <> - 2  AND T0."CANCELED" IN ('Y','N');

-- - Título: Relatorio de notas carrefour - (0230)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de notas carrefour - (0230).
SELECT       T0."DocNum" as "Nro doc SAP",     T0."Serial" as "Nro Nota fiscal",     'DS' AS "Tipo nota fiscal",     T0."DocTotal" as "Valor",     T0."CardCode" as "Cl",     T1."AliasName" as "Nome fantasia da loja",     T0."DocStatus" as "Status do documento",     T0."DocTotal" - T0."PaidSum" as "Saldo em aberto",    CASE WHEN T0."BPLId" = 3 THEN 'JFC &NATURAL SALADS'  WHEN T0."BPLId" = 1 THEN 'JFC PRODUTOS AGRICOLAS' WHEN T0."BPLId" =5 THEN 'NATURAL FARMS' ELSE T3."BPLName"   END AS  "Filial",     T0."FatherCard" as "Parceiro consolidado",    T0."DocDate" as "Data lancamento"  FROM     ORIN T0  INNER JOIN OCRD T1 ON T0."CardCode" = T1."CardCode" INNER JOIN "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@SD_CADREDE"  T2 ON T1."U_SD_Rede" = T2."Code"     LEFT JOIN OBPL T3 ON T3."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE     T0."DocDate"  >= add_days(current_date, -240)  AND  T0."DocDate"  <=current_date AND T0."CANCELED" = 'N'  AND (T2."Code" IN ('RJ569', 'RJ323', 'SP851', 'RJ254','PE004','RJ241') or T0."CardCode" in ('CL000987','CL004724','CL004723','CL000973','CL001013','CL001014','CL000975','CL000976','CL000974')) AND T0."SeriesStr" !='0' AND T0."SeriesStr" != ' '    UNION ALL  SELECT       T0."DocNum" as "Nro doc SAP",     T0."Serial" as "Nro Nota",     'NS' AS "Tipo nota fiscal",     T0."DocTotal" as "Valor",     T0."CardCode" as "Cl",     T1."AliasName" as "Nome fantasia da loja",     T0."DocStatus" as "Status do documento",     T0."DocTotal" - T0."PaidSum" as "Saldo em aberto",    CASE WHEN T0."BPLId" = 3 THEN 'JFC &NATURAL SALADS'  WHEN T0."BPLId" = 1 THEN 'JFC PRODUTOS AGRICOLAS' WHEN T0."BPLId" =5 THEN 'NATURAL FARMS' ELSE T3."BPLName"   END AS  "Filial",     T0."FatherCard" as "Parceiro consolidado",    T0."DocDate" as "Data lancamento"  FROM     OINV T0  INNER JOIN OCRD T1 ON T0."CardCode" = T1."CardCode" INNER JOIN "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@SD_CADREDE"  T2 ON T1."U_SD_Rede" = T2."Code"     LEFT JOIN OBPL T3 ON T3."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE     T0."DocDate"  >= add_days(current_date, -240)  AND  T0."DocDate"  <=current_date AND T0."CANCELED" = 'N'  AND (T2."Code" IN ('RJ569', 'RJ323', 'SP851', 'RJ254','PE004','RJ241') or T0."CardCode" in ('CL000987','CL004724','CL004723','CL000973','CL001013','CL001014','CL000975','CL000976','CL000974')) AND T0."SeriesStr" !='0' AND T0."SeriesStr" != ' ';

-- - Título: Relatorio de notas com saldo em aberto - (0234)

SELECT T0."DocNum", T0."Serial", T0."BPLName", T0."DocTotal", T0."PaidToDate", T0."DocTotal"-T0."PaidToDate" AS "Valor em aberto" FROM OINV T0 WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."DocTotal"!= T0."PaidToDate";

-- - Título: Relatorio de notas de devolução de cancelamento fora do prazo - (0049)

"Footer"), T6."DocNum" as "Nro doc nota de saída base",T6."Serial" as "Nro de serie nota de saída base" ,T6."DocEntry"  FROM ORIN T0 INNER JOIN RIN12 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN RIN1 T5 ON T0."DocEntry" = T5."DocEntry" INNER JOIN OUSR T2 ON T0."UserSign" = T2."USERID"  INNER JOIN NFN1 T3 ON T0."SeqCode"  = T3."SeqCode"  INNER JOIN OBPL T4 ON T4."BPLId" = T0."BPLId"  LEFT JOIN OINV T6 ON T6."DocNum" = T5."BaseRef" WHERE T0."CANCELED" = 'N' and T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T4."BPLName" = [%3] AND T0."SeqCode" <> - 2;

-- - Título: Relatorio de notas de devolução de cancelamento fora do prazo - (0049)
