-- - Título: Relatorio de pedidos de compras realizados baseado no deposito 006 - (0188)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de pedidos de compras realizados baseado no deposito 006 - (0188).
SELECT T0."DocNum",T0."DocDate",T0."CardCode", T0."CardName", T1."ItemCode",T2."ItemName",T3."ItmsGrpNam", T1."Quantity",  T1."PriceBefDi", T1."LineTotal", T1."WhsCode", T0."BPLName"  FROM OPOR T0   INNER JOIN POR1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" INNER JOIN OITB T3 ON T2."ItmsGrpCod" = T3."ItmsGrpCod"  WHERE (T1."WhsCode"  LIKE '%%6' OR T0."CardCode"  IN ('FO003369','FO001104','FO002591')) AND T0."BPLName"  = [%1] AND T0."DocDate">=[%2] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%3];

-- - Título: Relatorio de preço médio compra IL por pedido MP (Legumes e veduras) Bonito - (0113)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de preço médio compra il por pedido mp (legumes e veduras) bonito - (0113).
SELECT T3."ItemCode", T3."ItemName",T4."ItmsGrpNam",T3."InvntryUom",sum(T1."Quantity" * T2."NumInBuy") as "Quantidade na unidade de estoque",sum(T1."LineTotal") as "Valor Total Pago R$",sum(T1."LineTotal")/sum(T1."Quantity" * T2."NumInBuy") as "Preço médio calculado R$", 'Item de ligação' as "Tipo" FROM OPOR T0   INNER JOIN POR1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITM T3 ON T3."ItemCode" = T2."ValidComm" LEFT JOIN OITB T4 ON T4."ItmsGrpCod" = T3."ItmsGrpCod"   WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T1."Usage" in (19,47) AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] and T2."ItmsGrpCod" in (119,122) AND T3."ItemCode" LIKE '%IL%' AND T0."BPLId" in (1,9)  and T0."CardCode" NOT IN ('FO001340','FO002947','FO002087')  GROUP BY T3."InvntryUom",T3."ItemCode", T3."ItemName",T4."ItmsGrpNam"   UNION ALL  SELECT T3."ItemCode", T3."ItemName",T4."ItmsGrpNam",T3."InvntryUom",sum(T1."Quantity" * T3."NumInBuy") as "Quantidade na unidade de estoque",sum(T1."LineTotal") as "Valor Total Pago R$",sum(T1."LineTotal")/sum(T1."Quantity" * T3."NumInBuy") as "Preço médio calculado R$",'Embalado' as "Tipo" FROM OPOR T0   INNER JOIN POR1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OITM T3 ON T1."ItemCode" = T3."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITB T4 ON T3."ItmsGrpCod" = T4."ItmsGrpCod"   WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T1."Usage" in (19,47) AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] and (T3."ItmsGrpCod" in (123))  AND T0."BPLId" in (1,9)  and T0."CardCode" NOT IN ('FO001340','FO002947','FO002087')   GROUP BY  T3."ItemCode", T3."ItemName",T3."InvntryUom",T4."ItmsGrpNam"   UNION ALL SELECT T3."ItemCode", T3."ItemName",T4."ItmsGrpNam",T3."InvntryUom",sum(T1."Quantity" * T3."NumInBuy") as "Quantidade na unidade de estoque",sum(T1."LineTotal") as "Valor Total Pago R$",sum(T1."LineTotal")/sum(T1."Quantity" * T3."NumInBuy") as "Preço médio calculado R$",'Cogumelo' as "Tipo" FROM OPOR T0   INNER JOIN POR1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OITM T3 ON T1."ItemCode" = T3."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITB T4 ON T3."ItmsGrpCod" = T4."ItmsGrpCod"   WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T1."Usage" in (19,47) AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] and (T3."ItmsGrpCod" in (124))  AND T0."BPLId" in (1,9)  and T0."CardCode" NOT IN ('FO001340','FO002947','FO002087')   GROUP BY  T3."ItemCode", T3."ItemName",T3."InvntryUom",T4."ItmsGrpNam"  order BY T4."ItmsGrpNam",T3."ItemName";

-- - Título: Relatorio de preço médio compra IL por pedido MP (Legumes e veduras) Teresópolis- (0112)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de preço médio compra il por pedido mp (legumes e veduras) teresópolis- (0112).
SELECT T3."ItemCode", T3."ItemName",T4."ItmsGrpNam",T3."InvntryUom",sum(T1."Quantity" * T2."NumInBuy") as "Quantidade na unidade de estoque",sum(T1."LineTotal") as "Valor Total Pago R$",sum(T1."LineTotal")/sum(T1."Quantity" * T2."NumInBuy") as "Preço médio calculado R$", 'Item de ligação' as "Tipo" FROM OPOR T0   INNER JOIN POR1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITM T3 ON T3."ItemCode" = T2."ValidComm" LEFT JOIN OITB T4 ON T4."ItmsGrpCod" = T3."ItmsGrpCod"   WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T1."Usage" in (19,47) AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] and T2."ItmsGrpCod" in (119,122) AND T3."ItemCode" LIKE '%IL%' AND T0."BPLId" in (3,4,6,10)  and T0."CardCode" NOT IN ('FO001340','FO002947','FO002087')  GROUP BY T3."InvntryUom",T3."ItemCode", T3."ItemName",T4."ItmsGrpNam"   UNION ALL  SELECT T3."ItemCode", T3."ItemName",T4."ItmsGrpNam",T3."InvntryUom",sum(T1."Quantity" * T3."NumInBuy") as "Quantidade na unidade de estoque",sum(T1."LineTotal") as "Valor Total Pago R$",sum(T1."LineTotal")/sum(T1."Quantity" * T3."NumInBuy") as "Preço médio calculado R$",'Embalado' as "Tipo" FROM OPOR T0   INNER JOIN POR1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OITM T3 ON T1."ItemCode" = T3."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITB T4 ON T3."ItmsGrpCod" = T4."ItmsGrpCod"   WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T1."Usage" in (19,47) AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] and (T3."ItmsGrpCod" in (123))  AND T0."BPLId" in (3,4,6,10)  and T0."CardCode" NOT IN ('FO001340','FO002947','FO002087')   GROUP BY  T3."ItemCode", T3."ItemName",T3."InvntryUom",T4."ItmsGrpNam"   UNION ALL SELECT T3."ItemCode", T3."ItemName",T4."ItmsGrpNam",T3."InvntryUom",sum(T1."Quantity" * T3."NumInBuy") as "Quantidade na unidade de estoque",sum(T1."LineTotal") as "Valor Total Pago R$",sum(T1."LineTotal")/sum(T1."Quantity" * T3."NumInBuy") as "Preço médio calculado R$",'Cogumelo' as "Tipo" FROM OPOR T0   INNER JOIN POR1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OITM T3 ON T1."ItemCode" = T3."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITB T4 ON T3."ItmsGrpCod" = T4."ItmsGrpCod"   WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T1."Usage" in (19,47) AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] and (T3."ItmsGrpCod" in (124))  AND T0."BPLId" in (3,4,6,10)  and T0."CardCode" NOT IN ('FO001340','FO002947','FO002087')   GROUP BY  T3."ItemCode", T3."ItemName",T3."InvntryUom",T4."ItmsGrpNam"  order BY T4."ItmsGrpNam",T3."ItemName";

-- - Título: Relatorio de rastreamento de solicitações de compras - (0266)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de rastreamento de solicitações de compras - (0266).
SELECT  T0."DocNum"       AS "Numero_SC", TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocDate", 'DD/MM/YYYY')    AS "Data_SC", TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocDueDate", 'DD/MM/YYYY') AS "Data_Necessidade_SC", T11."BPLName", T1."ItemCode"     AS "Codigo_Item_SC", T2."ItemName"     AS "Descricao_Item_SC", T1."Quantity"     AS "Quantidade_SC", T1."WhsCode"      AS "Deposito_SC",  T4."DocNum"       AS "Numero_Oferta", T12."SlpName"     AS "Comprador_Oferta", T4."CardCode"     AS "Codigo_Fornecedor_Oferta", T4."CardName"     AS "Nome_Fornecedor_Oferta", TO_VARCHAR(T4."DocDate", 'DD/MM/YYYY')    AS "Data_Oferta", T3."Quantity"     AS "Quantidade_Oferta", T3."PriceBefDi"   AS "Preco_Oferta",  T6."DocNum"       AS "Numero_Pedido", T6."CardCode"     AS "Codigo_Fornecedor_Pedido", T13."SlpName"     AS "Comprador_Pedido", T6."CardName"     AS "Nome_Fornecedor_Pedido", TO_VARCHAR(T6."DocDate", 'DD/MM/YYYY')    AS "Data_Pedido", T5."Quantity"     AS "Quantidade_Pedido", T5."PriceBefDi"   AS "Preco_Pedido",  T8."DocNum"       AS "Numero_Recebimento", T8."CardCode"     AS "Codigo_Fornecedor_Recebimento", T8."CardName"     AS "Nome_Fornecedor_Recebimento", TO_VARCHAR(T8."DocDate", 'DD/MM/YYYY')    AS "Data_Recebimento", T7."Quantity"     AS "Quantidade_Recebimento", T7."PriceBefDi"   AS "Preco_Recebimento",  T10."DocNum"      AS "Numero_Nota", T10."CardCode"    AS "Codigo_Fornecedor_Nota", T10."CardName"    AS "Nome_Fornecedor_Nota", TO_VARCHAR(T10."DocDate", 'DD/MM/YYYY')   AS "Data_Nota", T9."Quantity"     AS "Quantidade_Nota", T9."PriceBefDi"   AS "Preco_Nota", T6."U_ObservacaoCompra"  FROM OPRQ T0   INNER JOIN PRQ1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN PQT1 T3 ON TO_VARCHAR(T3."BaseRef") = TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum")                     AND T3."LineNum" = T1."LineNum"  LEFT JOIN OPQT T4 ON T4."DocEntry" = T3."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN POR1 T5 ON TO_VARCHAR(T5."BaseRef") = TO_VARCHAR(COALESCE(T4."DocNum", T0."DocNum"))                      AND T5."BaseLine" = COALESCE(T3."LineNum",T1."LineNum")                    AND T5."BaseType" = COALESCE(T4."ObjType",T0."ObjType")                    AND T5."ItemCode" = COALESCE(T3."ItemCode",T1."ItemCode") LEFT JOIN OPOR T6 ON T6."DocEntry" = T5."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN PDN1 T7 ON TO_VARCHAR(T7."BaseRef") = TO_VARCHAR(T6."DocNum")                      AND T7."BaseLine" = T5."LineNum" LEFT JOIN OPDN T8 ON T8."DocEntry" = T7."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN PCH1 T9 ON TO_VARCHAR(T9."BaseRef") = TO_VARCHAR(COALESCE(T8."DocNum", T6."DocNum"))                       AND T9."BaseLine" = COALESCE(T7."LineNum", T5."LineNum")                      AND T9."BaseType" = COALESCE(T8."ObjType",T6."ObjType") LEFT JOIN OPCH T10 ON T10."DocEntry" = T9."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OBPL T11 ON T11."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" LEFT JOIN OSLP T12 ON T12."SlpCode" = T4."SlpCode"  LEFT JOIN OSLP T13 ON T13."SlpCode" = T6."SlpCode"   WHERE T0."DocDate">=[%1] and T0."DocDate"<=[%2]  AND (T4."CANCELED" ='N' OR T4."CANCELED" IS NULL)  AND (T6."CANCELED" ='N' OR T6."CANCELED" IS NULL)   AND (T8."CANCELED" ='N' OR T8."CANCELED" IS NULL)   AND (T10."CANCELED" ='N' OR T10."CANCELED" IS NULL)  ORDER BY T2."ItemName",T4."CardName";

-- - Título: Relatorio de recebimentos feitos pela service layer em aberto - (0291)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de recebimentos feitos pela service layer em aberto - (0291).
SELECT T0."DocNum", T0."DocDate", T0."CardCode", T0."CardName", T0."DocTotal" FROM OPDN T0 WHERE T0."UserSign" = 213 AND T0."DocStatus" ='O' AND T0."CANCELED" ='N';

-- - Título: Relatorio de recebimentos realizados de Teresopolis - (0236)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de recebimentos realizados de teresopolis - (0236).
SELECT T0."DocNum", T0."TaxDate", T2."CardCode", T2."CardName", T3."ItemCode", T3."ItemName", T4."ItmsGrpNam",T1."Quantity", T1."OpenQty", T1."PriceBefDi", case WHEN   T1."LineStatus" ='O'  AND T1."OpenQty"<T1."Quantity" THEN 'ABERTO PARCIALMENTE' WHEN T1."LineStatus" ='C' THEN 'FECHADO' WHEN T1."LineStatus" ='O'  AND T1."OpenQty"=T1."Quantity" THEN 'ABERTO' END AS "STATUS DA LINHA" FROM OPDN T0  INNER JOIN PDN1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" INNER JOIN OCRD T2 ON T0."CardCode" = T2."CardCode" INNER JOIN OITM T3 ON T1."ItemCode" = T3."ItemCode" INNER JOIN OITB T4 ON T3."ItmsGrpCod" = T4."ItmsGrpCod" WHERE T0."BPLId" in (3,4,6,10) AND T1."Usage" in (19,47) AND T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."TaxDate">=[%1] AND T0."TaxDate"<=[%2]  AND T0."U_NotaAjusteInterno" ='N' AND T3."ItmsGrpCod" IN (119,122,123,131);

-- - Título: Relatorio de redes para pesquisa dinamica no campo U_RefRedeCliente - (0084)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de redes para pesquisa dinamica no campo u_refredecliente - (0084).
SELECT T0."Code"|| '-' || T0."Name" as "Pk-Rede", T0."Code", T0."Name"  FROM "@SD_CADREDE" T0 WHERE T0."Code" <> 'DESATIVADO';

-- - Título: Relatorio de saldo inicial RECIFE - (0123)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de saldo inicial recife - (0123).
SELECT T0."CreateDate", T1."ItemCode", T1."ItemName", T3."ItmsGrpNam",T1."WhsCode",T1."Quantity",  T1."Price", T1."DocTotal", T0."BPLName" FROM OIQI T0 INNER JOIN  IQI1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" INNER JOIN OITB T3 ON T2."ItmsGrpCod" = T3."ItmsGrpCod" WHERE T0."BPLId"  IN (1,9);

-- - Título: Relatorio de saída de itens da oficina - (0196)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de saída de itens da oficina - (0196).
SELECT T0."DocDate", T2."ItemCode", T1."Dscription", T1."WhsCode", T1."Quantity", T1."StockPrice",T1."Quantity" * T1."StockPrice" as "TOTAL R$", T1."U_KM_HORA", T1."U_Equipamento_Veiculo", T1."U_Solicitante",T0."Comments" FROM OIGE T0  INNER JOIN IGE1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OITM T2 ON T2."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode" WHERE T1."WhsCode"  LIKE '%%08' AND  T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."TaxDate" >= [%1] AND T0."TaxDate"<=[%2]  ORDER BY T0."DocDate" DESC, T1."Dscription";

-- - Título: Relatorio de saída de itens da oficina - (0196)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de saída de itens da oficina - (0196).
SELECT T0."DocDate", T2."ItemCode", T1."Dscription", T1."WhsCode", T1."Quantity", T1."StockPrice",T1."Quantity" * T1."StockPrice" as "TOTAL R$", T1."U_KM_HORA", T1."U_Equipamento_Veiculo", T1."U_Solicitante",T0."Comments" FROM OIGE T0  INNER JOIN IGE1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OITM T2 ON T2."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode" WHERE T1."WhsCode"  LIKE '%%08' AND  T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."TaxDate" >= [%1] AND T0."TaxDate"<=[%2]  ORDER BY T0."DocDate" DESC, T1."Dscription";

-- - Título: Relatorio de saídas de itens  SAP - (0324)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de saídas de itens  sap - (0324).
SELECT T0."DocNum",  T0."DocDate", T0."TaxDate",T0."CardCode", T0."CardName", T1."ItemCode", T2."ItemName", T1."Quantity", T1."PriceBefDi", T1."LineTotal", T1."WhsCode", T0."Comments" FROM OIGE T0  INNER JOIN IGE1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" WHERE T1."ItemCode" ='001945';

-- - Título: Relatorio de supervisores comissionados - (0310)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de supervisores comissionados - (0310).
WITH CTE AS (SELECT  T0."DocEntry" as "Pk documento", T0."DocNum", T0."Serial" as "Nro da nota fiscal",  T0."DocDate", T0."CardCode" AS "Pk codigo do PN", T0."DiscSum" as "Desconto do documento", T0."DiscPrcnt" as " % Desconto no documento", T0."DocTotal",  T0."BPLId" as "Pk filial",  T1."ItemCode",  T1."Quantity", T1."PriceBefDi" as "Preco antes do desconto R$",  T1."Price" AS "Preco apos desconto", T1."LineTotal", T1."Usage" as "Pk utilizacao", T0."U_NotaAjusteInterno"   FROM OPCH T0  INNER JOIN PCH1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITB T3 ON T2."ItmsGrpCod" = T3."ItmsGrpCod"   WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T1."Usage" =50  AND  T3."ItmsGrpCod" IN (119,120,121,122,123,124,125,131,137)), cte2 as (  SELECT  CASE WHEN (SELECT distinct T00."CardCode" as "Codigo Pn" FROM CRD7 T00 WHERE T00."CardCode" LIKE 'CL%' AND T00."TaxId0" = T1."TaxId0" AND T00."TaxId0"  IS NOT NULL  ) IS NULL THEN T0."Pk codigo do PN" ELSE (SELECT distinct T00."CardCode" as "Codigo Pn" FROM CRD7 T00 WHERE T00."CardCode" LIKE 'CL%' AND T00."TaxId0" = T1."TaxId0" ) END  as "CardCode", T0."ItemCode" , T0."LineTotal"  FROM CTE  T0 LEFT JOIN PCH12 T1 ON T1."DocEntry" = T0."Pk documento")   SELECT  T0."U_CardCode",  T3."CardName", T3."AliasName" as "Nome fantasia", T1."U_CodSupervisor",  T1."U_NomeSupervisor", T1."U_CodGrupoItens",  T1."U_NomeGrupoItens",  T1."U_Periodo",  T1."U_CodFechamento",  T1."U_StatusLinha" ,  (SELECT  SUM(T01."LineTotal" )  FROM OINV T00 INNER JOIN INV1 T01 ON T01."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OITM T02 ON T02."ItemCode" = T01."ItemCode"  WHERE T00."CANCELED" ='N'  AND T01."Usage" in (15,74) AND T00."DocDate">=[%1] AND T00."DocDate"<=[%2]  AND T0."U_CardCode" = T00."CardCode" AND T02."ItmsGrpCod"  = T1."U_CodGrupoItens"  ) as "Faturamento R$" , (SELECT  SUM(T01."LineTotal" )  FROM ORIN T00 INNER JOIN RIN1 T01 ON T01."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OITM T02 ON T02."ItemCode" = T01."ItemCode"  WHERE T00."CANCELED" ='N'  AND T01."Usage" in (15,74) AND T00."DocDate">=[%1] AND T00."DocDate"<=[%2]  AND T0."U_CardCode" = T00."CardCode" AND T02."ItmsGrpCod"  = T1."U_CodGrupoItens"  ) as "Devolução R$", (SELECT  SUM(T00."LineTotal" )  FROM cte2 T00 LEFT JOIN OITM T02 ON T02."ItemCode" = T00."ItemCode"  WHERE T0."U_CardCode" = T00."CardCode"  AND  T02."ItmsGrpCod"  = T1."U_CodGrupoItens" ) as "Devolução PAGA R$"  FROM "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@COMISSIONADOS_HEAD"  T0  LEFT JOIN "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@COMISSIONADOS_LINHA"  T1 ON T1."DocEntry"= T0."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OCRD T3 ON T3."CardCode" = T0."U_CardCode" ORDER BY T3."CardName",T1."U_NomeSupervisor" ASC;

-- - Título: Relatorio de transferencias de estoque - (0267)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de transferencias de estoque - (0267).
SELECT T0."DocNum", T3."BPLName",T0."DocDate", T2."ItemCode", T2."ItemName", T1."Quantity",T1."FromWhsCod",  T1."WhsCode" FROM OWTR T0   INNER JOIN WTR1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OBPL T3 ON T3."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2];

-- - Título: Relatorio de ultimas notas emitidas com data de saída - (0249)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de ultimas notas emitidas com data de saída - (0249).
with  cte as (SELECT T0."DocNum", T0."DocDate",  T1."U_NAME", T0."CreateDate", T0."CreateTS",T0."U_TX_DtSaid", TO_VARCHAR((SELECT MAX(T00."DateReturn") FROM  "DBInvOne"."Process" T000 INNER JOIN "DBInvOne"."ProcessHist" T00 ON T00."KeyNfe" = T000."KeyNfe"  WHERE T00."ReturnId"  =100 AND T000."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry" AND T000."DocType"  = 13) , 'DD/MM/YYYY') AS "Data de autorização da NF", TO_VARCHAR((SELECT MAX(T00."DateReturn") FROM  "DBInvOne"."Process" T000 INNER JOIN "DBInvOne"."ProcessHist" T00 ON T00."KeyNfe" = T000."KeyNfe"  WHERE T00."ReturnId"  =100 AND T000."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry" AND T000."DocType"  = 13) , 'HH24:MI:SS') AS "Hora de autorização da NF" FROM OINV T0  INNER JOIN OUSR T1 ON T0."UserSign" = T1."USERID"  WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND TO_DATE(COALESCE(TO_DATE(T0."U_TX_DtSaid"), T0."DocDate"))>='2025-12-01' AND T0."UserSign" in (220,90,85,207,116,208,219) AND T0."CardCode" NOT IN ('CL000581', 'CL004167')),  CTE2 AS (   SELECT     "Data de entrega",     TO_VARCHAR(       "Data_hora_autorizacao",       'DD/MM/YYYY HH24:MI:SS'     ) AS "Data_hora_autorizacao"   FROM (     SELECT       COALESCE(TO_DATE(t00."U_TX_DtSaid"), t00."DocDate") AS "Data de entrega",        TO_TIMESTAMP(         t00."Data de autorização da NF" || ' ' || t00."Hora de autorização da NF",         'DD/MM/YYYY HH24:MI:SS'       ) AS "Data_hora_autorizacao",        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (         PARTITION BY COALESCE(TO_DATE(t00."U_TX_DtSaid"), t00."DocDate")         ORDER BY           /* 1️⃣ prioridade: madrugada */           CASE            WHEN  WEEKDAY(  TO_TIMESTAMP(         t00."Data de autorização da NF" || ' ' || t00."Hora de autorização da NF",         'DD/MM/YYYY HH24:MI:SS'       ) )= 6 AND TO_TIME(t00."Hora de autorização da NF")>= TIME '18:30:00' OR TO_TIME(t00."Hora de autorização da NF") <='05:30:00' THEN 1              WHEN TO_TIME(t00."Hora de autorização da NF")                  BETWEEN TIME '00:00:00' AND TIME '05:30:00' AND WEEKDAY(  TO_TIMESTAMP(         t00."Data de autorização da NF" || ' ' || t00."Hora de autorização da NF",         'DD/MM/YYYY HH24:MI:SS'       ) ) <>6             THEN 1             ELSE 2           END,           /* 2️⃣ dentro da madrugada → mais próximo de 05:30 */           CASE             WHEN TO_TIME(t00."Hora de autorização da NF")                  BETWEEN TIME '00:00:00' AND TIME '05:30:00' AND WEEKDAY(  TO_TIMESTAMP(         t00."Data de autorização da NF" || ' ' || t00."Hora de autorização da NF",         'DD/MM/YYYY HH24:MI:SS'       ) ) <>6             THEN TO_TIME(t00."Hora de autorização da NF")           END DESC,           /* 3️⃣ senão → maior horário do dia */           TO_TIME(t00."Hora de autorização da NF") DESC       ) AS RN      FROM cte t00     WHERE       (         TO_TIME(t00."Hora de autorização da NF") <= TIME '05:30:00'         OR TO_TIME(t00."Hora de autorização da NF") >= TIME '18:30:00'       )       AND t00."U_TX_DtSaid" IS NOT NULL   )   WHERE RN = 1 ) select t0."Data de entrega",TO_DATE(t0."Data_hora_autorizacao", 'DD/MM/YYYY HH24:MI:SS') AS "Data autorização", SUBSTRING(t0."Data_hora_autorizacao", 12, 8) AS "Hora da autorização" from CTE2 t0  ORDER BY TO_DATE(t0."Data_hora_autorizacao", 'DD/MM/YYYY HH24:MI:SS'), SUBSTRING(t0."Data_hora_autorizacao", 12, 8);

-- - Título: Relatorio de ultimos precos para contabilizacao de cortes - (0257)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de ultimos precos para contabilizacao de cortes - (0257).
WITH UltimoPreco AS (     SELECT         T00."CardCode",         T01."ItemCode",         T01."PriceBefDi",         ROW_NUMBER() OVER (             PARTITION BY T00."CardCode", T01."ItemCode"             ORDER BY T00."DocNum" DESC         ) AS RN     FROM OINV T00     INNER JOIN INV1 T01          ON T01."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry"     WHERE          T00."CANCELED" = 'N'         AND T01."Usage" = 15 ), ITEN_DEVOLUCAO AS (  SELECT     T0."Code",     T0."Name",     T1."U_ItemCode",     UP."PriceBefDi" AS "LastPrice" FROM "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@SD_ITEM_CLI" T0 LEFT JOIN "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@SD_ITEM_CLI_1" T1      ON T1."Code" = T0."Code" LEFT JOIN UltimoPreco UP     ON UP."CardCode" = T0."Code"     AND UP."ItemCode" = T1."U_ItemCode"     AND UP.RN = 1 )  SELECT T0."Code",     T0."Name",     T0."U_ItemCode",     T0."LastPrice" AS "Ultimo Preco",     COALESCE(T0."LastPrice", (SELECT MAX(T00."LastPrice") FROM ITEN_DEVOLUCAO T00 WHERE T0."U_ItemCode"  = T00."U_ItemCode")) AS "Ultimo preço calculado caso ocorra venda"   FROM ITEN_DEVOLUCAO T0;

-- - Título: Relatorio de usuários e seus grupos de autorizações - (0043)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de usuários e seus grupos de autorizações - (0043).
SELECT T0."USER_CODE", T0."U_NAME", T0."E_Mail",  T2."GroupName", T2."GroupDec"FROM OUSR T0  INNER JOIN USR7 T1 ON T0."USERID" = T1."UserId" INNER JOIN OUGR T2 ON T1."GroupId" = T2."GroupId" WHERE T0."Locked" ='N' ORDER BY  T2."GroupName",T0."USER_CODE";

-- - Título: Relatorio de vendas e devolução manoel - (0327)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de vendas e devolução manoel - (0327).
SELECT MONTH(T0."DocDate") || '/' || YEAR(T0."DocDate") AS "Periodo",T1."BPLName",sum(T0."DocTotal") as "Valor R$",  'VENDA' AS "TIPO"   FROM OINV T0  INNER JOIN OBPL T1 ON T0."BPLId" = T1."BPLId" WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."BPLId" in (9,6) GROUP BY MONTH(T0."DocDate") || '/' || YEAR(T0."DocDate"),T1."BPLName"  UNION ALL  SELECT MONTH(T0."DocDate") || '/' || YEAR(T0."DocDate") AS "Periodo",T1."BPLName",sum(T0."DocTotal") as "Valor R$",  'DEVOLUÇÃO DE VENDA' AS "TIPO"   FROM ORIN T0  INNER JOIN OBPL T1 ON T0."BPLId" = T1."BPLId" WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."BPLId" in (9,6)   GROUP BY MONTH(T0."DocDate") || '/' || YEAR(T0."DocDate"),T1."BPLName";

-- - Título: Relatorio de vendas e devolução manoel detalhado- (0330)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de vendas e devolução manoel detalhado- (0330).
SELECT     T0."DocNum",     T10."NfmName" AS "Modelo",     T0."DocDate",     T0."Serial" AS "Número nota fiscal",     T0."CardCode",     T0."CardName",     T0."DocTotal",     T1."BPLName",     T0."DocTotal",     'VENDA' AS "TIPO",      T2."LineNum",     COALESCE(T2."ItemCode", T5."AcctCode") AS "Codigo do item/Conta",     COALESCE(T4."ItemName", T5."AcctName") AS "Nome do item/Conta",     T2."PriceBefDi",     T2."Quantity",     T2."LineTotal",     T3."Usage",    STRING_AGG(     CASE          WHEN T01."Debit" > 0          THEN T01."Account"     END,     ' | '   ) AS "Codigos contas movimentadas A DEBITO",    STRING_AGG(     CASE          WHEN T01."Debit" > 0          THEN T01."Account" || ' ' || T02."AcctName"     END,     ' | '   ) AS "Contas movimentadas A DEBITO", STRING_AGG(     CASE          WHEN T01."Credit" > 0          THEN T01."Account"      END,     ' | ' ) AS "Codigos contas movimentadas A CREDITO", STRING_AGG(     CASE          WHEN T01."Credit" > 0          THEN T01."Account" || ' ' || T02."AcctName"     END,     ' | ' ) AS "Contas movimentadas A CREDITO" FROM OINV T0 INNER JOIN OBPL T1     ON T0."BPLId" = T1."BPLId" LEFT JOIN INV1 T2     ON T2."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OUSG T3     ON T3."ID" = T2."Usage" LEFT JOIN OITM T4     ON T4."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OACT T5     ON T5."AcctCode" = T2."AcctCode" LEFT JOIN OJDT T00 ON  TO_VARCHAR(T00."BaseRef") = TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum") AND T00."TransType" = 13 LEFT JOIN JDT1 T01 ON T00."TransId" = T01."TransId"  LEFT JOIN OACT T02 ON T02."AcctCode" = T01."Account" LEFT JOIN ONFM T10 ON T0."Model" = T10."AbsEntry"  WHERE T0."CANCELED" = 'N'  AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2]    AND T0."BPLId" IN (9,6) GROUP BY      T0."DocNum",     T0."DocDate",     T10."NfmName",     T0."Serial",     T0."CardCode",     T0."CardName",     T0."DocTotal",     T1."BPLName",     T0."DocTotal", T2."LineNum",     COALESCE(T2."ItemCode", T5."AcctCode"),     COALESCE(T4."ItemName", T5."AcctName"),     T2."PriceBefDi",     T2."Quantity",     T2."LineTotal",     T3."Usage"  UNION ALL  SELECT     T0."DocNum",     T10."NfmName",     T0."DocDate",     T0."Serial" AS "Número nota fiscal",     T0."CardCode",     T0."CardName",     T0."DocTotal",     T1."BPLName",     T0."DocTotal",     'DEVOLUÇÃO DE VENDA' AS "TIPO", T2."LineNum",     COALESCE(T2."ItemCode", T5."AcctCode") AS "Codigo do item/Conta",     COALESCE(T4."ItemName", T5."AcctName") AS "Nome do item/Conta",     T2."PriceBefDi",     T2."Quantity",     T2."LineTotal",     T3."Usage",    STRING_AGG(     CASE          WHEN T01."Debit" > 0          THEN T01."Account"     END,     ' | '   ) AS "Codigos contas movimentadas A DEBITO", STRING_AGG(     CASE          WHEN T01."Debit" > 0          THEN T01."Account" || ' ' || T02."AcctName"     END,     ' | ' ) AS "Contas movimentadas A DEBITO", STRING_AGG(     CASE          WHEN T01."Credit" > 0          THEN T01."Account"      END,     ' | ' ) AS "Codigos contas movimentadas A CREDITO", STRING_AGG(     CASE          WHEN T01."Credit" > 0          THEN T01."Account" || ' ' || T02."AcctName"     END,     ' | ' ) AS "Contas movimentadas A CREDITO" FROM ORIN T0 INNER JOIN OBPL T1     ON T0."BPLId" = T1."BPLId" LEFT JOIN RIN1 T2     ON T2."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OUSG T3     ON T3."ID" = T2."Usage" LEFT JOIN OITM T4     ON T4."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OACT T5     ON T5."AcctCode" = T2."AcctCode" LEFT JOIN OJDT T00 ON  TO_VARCHAR(T00."BaseRef") = TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocNum") AND T00."TransType" = 14 LEFT JOIN JDT1 T01 ON T00."TransId" = T01."TransId" LEFT JOIN OACT T02 ON T02."AcctCode" = T01."Account" LEFT JOIN ONFM T10 ON T0."Model" = T10."AbsEntry" WHERE T0."CANCELED" = 'N'   AND T0."BPLId" IN (9,6) AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2]   GROUP BY      T0."DocNum",     T10."NfmName",     T0."DocDate",     T0."Serial",     T0."CardCode",     T0."CardName",     T0."DocTotal",     T1."BPLName",     T0."DocTotal",     T2."LineNum",     COALESCE(T2."ItemCode", T5."AcctCode"),     COALESCE(T4."ItemName", T5."AcctName"),     T2."PriceBefDi",     T2."Quantity",     T2."LineTotal",     T3."Usage";

-- - Título: Relatorio de verificação de canhotos entregues (RECIFE) - (0158)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de verificação de canhotos entregues (recife) - (0158).
SELECT DISTINCT  T0."DocNum",  T0."CardCode",  TO_VARCHAR(T2."AliasName") as "Nome fantasia",  T0."DocDate",  T0."U_TX_DtSaid",  T4."BPLName",  T0."Serial",  CASE WHEN T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido" ='N' THEN 'SEM CANHOTO' ELSE 'COM CANHOTO' END AS "CANHOTO",  T0."U_SDDataCanhoto" ,  T3."SlpName", T0."U_WB_RouteNumber" as "Código da Rota", T5."Name" as "Nome da rota", T0."DocTotal" FROM OINV T0   INNER JOIN INV1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" INNER JOIN OCRD T2 ON T0."CardCode" = T2."CardCode"  INNER JOIN OSLP T3 ON T0."SlpCode" = T3."SlpCode"  INNER JOIN OBPL T4 ON T0."BPLId" = T4."BPLId"  LEFT JOIN "@SD_ROTA" T5 ON T5."Code" = T0."U_WB_RouteNumber"  WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."BPLId" in (1,9) AND T1."Usage" IN (15,18) AND T0."DocStatus" ='O';

-- - Título: Relatorio de verificação de canhotos entregues (RECIFE) -com data- (0271)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de verificação de canhotos entregues (recife) -com data- (0271).
WITH NOTAS AS ( SELECT DISTINCT  T0."DocNum",  T0."CardCode",  TO_VARCHAR(T2."AliasName") as "Nome fantasia",  T0."DocDate",  T0."U_TX_DtSaid",  T4."BPLName",  T0."Serial",  CASE WHEN T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido" ='N' THEN 'SEM CANHOTO' ELSE 'COM CANHOTO' END AS "CANHOTO",  T0."U_SDDataCanhoto" ,  T3."SlpName", T0."U_WB_RouteNumber" as "Código da Rota", T5."Name" as "Nome da rota", T0."DocTotal" FROM OINV T0   INNER JOIN INV1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" INNER JOIN OCRD T2 ON T0."CardCode" = T2."CardCode"  INNER JOIN OSLP T3 ON T0."SlpCode" = T3."SlpCode"  INNER JOIN OBPL T4 ON T0."BPLId" = T4."BPLId"  LEFT JOIN "@SD_ROTA" T5 ON T5."Code" = T0."U_WB_RouteNumber"  WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."BPLId" in (1,9) AND T1."Usage" IN (15,18) AND T0."DocStatus" ='O' ), CTE AS ( SELECT T0."DocNum" as "Doc",T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido" AS "CANHOTO",T0."UpdateDate" AS "ULTIMA", T0.*   FROM ADOC T0 WHERE T0."DocNum"  IN (SELECT T00."DocNum" FROM NOTAS T00)  AND T0."ObjType" = 13 UNION ALL  SELECT T0."DocNum" as "Doc", T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido" AS "CANHOTO" ,T0."UpdateDate" AS  "ULTIMA", T0.* FROM OINV T0 WHERE T0."DocNum"  IN (SELECT T00."DocNum" FROM NOTAS T00))  SELECT * ,(SELECT MIN(T0."UpdateDate") FROM CTE T0 WHERE T0."U_SDCanhotoRecebido" ='Y' AND T00."DocNum" =T0."Doc" ) as "Data de entrada canhoto"  FROM NOTAS T00;

-- - Título: Relatorio de vinculo de CLS e suas rotas por dia da semana - (0176)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de vinculo de cls e suas rotas por dia da semana - (0176).
with cte as (SELECT T0."Code",T0."U_CardCode", T0."U_Segunda", T0."U_Terca", T0."U_Quarta", T0."U_Quinta", T0."U_Sexta", T0."U_Sabado", T0."U_Domingo"  FROM "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@SD_ROTA_CLI"  T0  LEFT JOIN  "SBO_GRUPOCAMPANHA_PRD"."@SD_ROTA"  T1 ON T1."Code"  = T0."Code"), ROTAS_SEGUNDA AS (     SELECT          T00."U_CardCode",         STRING_AGG(T00."Code", '-') AS "Rotas vinculado"     FROM "@SD_ROTA_CLI" T00     WHERE T00."U_Segunda" = 'Y'      GROUP BY T00."U_CardCode" ), ROTAS_TERCA AS (     SELECT          T00."U_CardCode",         STRING_AGG(T00."Code", '-') AS "Rotas vinculado"     FROM "@SD_ROTA_CLI" T00     WHERE T00."U_Terca" = 'Y'      GROUP BY T00."U_CardCode" ), ROTAS_QUARTA AS (     SELECT          T00."U_CardCode",         STRING_AGG(T00."Code", '-') AS "Rotas vinculado"     FROM "@SD_ROTA_CLI" T00     WHERE T00."U_Quarta" = 'Y'      GROUP BY T00."U_CardCode" ), ROTAS_QUINTA AS (     SELECT          T00."U_CardCode",         STRING_AGG(T00."Code", '-') AS "Rotas vinculado"     FROM "@SD_ROTA_CLI" T00     WHERE T00."U_Quinta" = 'Y'      GROUP BY T00."U_CardCode" ), ROTAS_SEXTA AS (     SELECT          T00."U_CardCode",         STRING_AGG(T00."Code", '-') AS "Rotas vinculado"     FROM "@SD_ROTA_CLI" T00     WHERE T00."U_Sexta" = 'Y'      GROUP BY T00."U_CardCode" ), ROTAS_SABADO AS (     SELECT          T00."U_CardCode",         STRING_AGG(T00."Code", '-') AS "Rotas vinculado"     FROM "@SD_ROTA_CLI" T00     WHERE T00."U_Sabado" = 'Y'      GROUP BY T00."U_CardCode" ), ROTAS_DOMINGO AS (     SELECT          T00."U_CardCode",         STRING_AGG(T00."Code", '-') AS "Rotas vinculado"     FROM "@SD_ROTA_CLI" T00     WHERE T00."U_Domingo" = 'Y'      GROUP BY T00."U_CardCode" )      SELECT  T0."CardCode",  T0."CardName",  (SELECT count(T00."U_Segunda") FROM "@SD_ROTA_CLI" T00 WHERE T00."U_CardCode" = T0."CardCode" AND T00."U_Segunda" = 'Y') as "SEGUNDA FEIRA" , (SELECT T000."Rotas vinculado" FROM "ROTAS_SEGUNDA" T000 WHERE T000."U_CardCode" = T0."CardCode") as "Rotas vinculadas:SEGUNDA FEIRA",  (SELECT count(T00."U_Terca") FROM "@SD_ROTA_CLI" T00 WHERE T00."U_CardCode" = T0."CardCode" AND  T00."U_Terca"= 'Y') as "TERÇA FEIRA" , (SELECT T000."Rotas vinculado" FROM "ROTAS_TERCA" T000 WHERE T000."U_CardCode" = T0."CardCode") as "Rotas vinculadas:TERÇA FEIRA",  (SELECT count(T00."U_Quarta") FROM "@SD_ROTA_CLI" T00 WHERE T00."U_CardCode" = T0."CardCode" AND  T00."U_Quarta"= 'Y') as "QUARTA FEIRA" , (SELECT T000."Rotas vinculado" FROM "ROTAS_QUARTA" T000 WHERE T000."U_CardCode" = T0."CardCode") as "Rotas vinculadas:QUARTA FEIRA",  (SELECT count(T00."U_Quinta") FROM "@SD_ROTA_CLI" T00 WHERE T00."U_CardCode" = T0."CardCode" AND T00."U_Quinta" = 'Y') as "QUINTA FEIRA" , (SELECT T000."Rotas vinculado" FROM "ROTAS_QUINTA" T000 WHERE T000."U_CardCode" = T0."CardCode") as "Rotas vinculadas:QUINTA FEIRA",  (SELECT count(T00."U_Sexta") FROM "@SD_ROTA_CLI" T00 WHERE T00."U_CardCode" = T0."CardCode" AND T00."U_Sexta" = 'Y') as "SEXTA FEIRA" , (SELECT T000."Rotas vinculado" FROM "ROTAS_SEXTA" T000 WHERE T000."U_CardCode" = T0."CardCode") as "Rotas vinculadas:SEXTA FEIRA",  (SELECT count(T00."U_Sabado") FROM "@SD_ROTA_CLI" T00 WHERE T00."U_CardCode" = T0."CardCode" AND T00."U_Sabado" = 'Y') as "SABADO" , (SELECT T000."Rotas vinculado" FROM "ROTAS_SABADO" T000 WHERE T000."U_CardCode" = T0."CardCode") as "Rotas vinculadas:SABADO",  (SELECT count(T00."U_Domingo") FROM "@SD_ROTA_CLI" T00 WHERE T00."U_CardCode" = T0."CardCode" AND  T00."U_Domingo"='Y') as "DOMINGO" , (SELECT T000."Rotas vinculado" FROM "ROTAS_DOMINGO" T000 WHERE T000."U_CardCode" = T0."CardCode") as "Rotas vinculadas:DOMINGO" FROM OCRD T0 where T0."CardCode" IN (SELECT T01."U_CardCode" FROM "@SD_ROTA_CLI" T01) ORDER BY T0."CardName" ASC;

-- - Título: Relatorio de último preço unitário pago na venda por CL - (0116)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio de último preço unitário pago na venda por cl - (0116).
SELECT T0."CardCode", T0."CardName",T2."ItemCode", T2."ItemName",T4."ItmsGrpNam",T2."InvntryUom", (SELECT distinct  T01."LineTotal"/T01."Quantity" FROM OINV T00 INNER JOIN INV1 T01 ON T01."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry" AND T00."DocNum" =  MAX(T0."DocNum") AND T01."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode") as "Ultimo preço unitário pago R$" FROM OINV T0   INNER JOIN INV1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode" LEFT JOIN OITB T4 ON T4."ItmsGrpCod" = T2."ItmsGrpCod"   WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T1."Usage" in (15) AND T0."DocDate">=add_days(current_date,-60) AND T0."DocDate"<=current_date and T0."BPLId" in (3,4,6,10)  and T0."CardCode" NOT IN ('CL001471','CL001482','CL001520','CL002158','CL003964','CL001264')  GROUP BY T0."CardCode", T0."CardName",T2."InvntryUom",T2."ItemCode", T2."ItemName",T4."ItmsGrpNam";

-- - Título: Relatorio ferramenta de comparativo DFE - (0148)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio ferramenta de comparativo dfe - (0148).
WITH CTE AS (SELECT T0."DocNum", T0."DocDate", T0."DocTotal", T0."Serial", T0."CardCode", T0."Comments",  (SELECT MAX(T00."DocEntry") FROM OPCH T00 LEFT JOIN PCH12 T01 ON T01."DocEntry"= T00."DocEntry" WHERE T00."CardCode"= T0."CardCode") as "Nota mais recente", T0."UserSign", T3."U_NAME", T4."BPLName", T4."BPLId",'NOTA FISCAL DE ENTRADA ' AS "Nota fiscal de entrada"  ,T1."FatherCard" as "PARCEIRO CONSOLIDADO" FROM OPCH T0   LEFT JOIN OCRD T1 ON T0."CardCode" = T1."CardCode"  INNER JOIN PCH12 T2 ON T0."DocEntry" = T2."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OUSR T3 ON T0."UserSign" = T3."USERID"  INNER JOIN OBPL T4 ON T0."BPLId" = T4."BPLId"  WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."Model" in (39,45)),CTE2 AS ( SELECT  T0."DocNum", T0."DocDate", T0."DocTotal", T0."Serial", T0."CardCode", T0."Comments",  CASE WHEN (SELECT max( T00."TaxId0")  FROM CRD7 T00 WHERE T00."CardCode" NOT LIKE 'CL%' AND T0."CardCode"= T00."CardCode" AND T00."TaxId0"  IS NOT NULL AND T00."TaxId0"  <> ''  ) IS NULL THEN   (SELECT MAX(T00."TaxId4")  FROM CRD7 T00 WHERE T00."CardCode" NOT LIKE 'CL%' AND T0."CardCode"= T00."CardCode" AND T00."TaxId4"  IS NOT NULL AND T00."TaxId4"  <> ''  ) ELSE (SELECT LEFT(MAX(T00."TaxId0"),10)  FROM CRD7 T00 WHERE T00."CardCode" NOT LIKE 'CL%' AND T0."CardCode"= T00."CardCode" AND T00."TaxId0"  IS NOT NULL  AND T00."TaxId0"  <> '' ) END AS "IDENTIFICAÇÃO" , T0."UserSign", T0."U_NAME", T0."BPLName", T0."BPLId",'NOTA FISCAL DE ENTRADA ' AS "Nota fiscal de entrada"  ,T0."PARCEIRO CONSOLIDADO"   FROM CTE T0)  SELECT *,T0."Serial"||'-'||T0."IDENTIFICAÇÃO"  as "CHAVE-PRIMARIA"  FROM CTE2 T0;

-- - Título: Relatorio ferramenta de comparativo DFE -V2 - (0160)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio ferramenta de comparativo dfe -v2 - (0160).
WITH CTE AS   (SELECT T0."DocNum",           T0."DocDate",           T0."DocTotal",           T0."Serial",           T0."CardCode",           T0."Comments",       (SELECT MAX(T00."DocEntry")       FROM OPCH T00       LEFT JOIN PCH12 T01 ON T01."DocEntry"= T00."DocEntry"       WHERE T00."CardCode"= T0."CardCode") AS "Nota mais recente",           T0."UserSign",           T3."U_NAME",           T4."BPLName",           T4."BPLId",           'NOTA FISCAL DE ENTRADA' AS "Tipo de documento" ,           T1."FatherCard" AS "PARCEIRO CONSOLIDADO"    FROM OPCH T0    LEFT JOIN OCRD T1 ON T0."CardCode" = T1."CardCode"    INNER JOIN PCH12 T2 ON T0."DocEntry" = T2."DocEntry"    INNER JOIN OUSR T3 ON T0."UserSign" = T3."USERID"    INNER JOIN OBPL T4 ON T0."BPLId" = T4."BPLId"    WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N'      AND T0."DocDate">=[%1]      AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2]      AND T0."Model" IN (39,                         45)),             CTE2 AS   (SELECT T0."DocNum",           T0."DocDate",           T0."DocTotal",           T0."Serial",           T0."CardCode",           T0."Comments",           CASE               WHEN                      (SELECT max(T00."TaxId0")                       FROM CRD7 T00                       WHERE T00."CardCode" NOT LIKE 'CL%'                         AND T0."CardCode"= T00."CardCode"                         AND T00."TaxId0" IS NOT NULL                         AND T00."TaxId0" <> '') IS NULL THEN                      (SELECT MAX(T00."TaxId4")                       FROM CRD7 T00                       WHERE T00."CardCode" NOT LIKE 'CL%'                         AND T0."CardCode"= T00."CardCode"                         AND T00."TaxId4" IS NOT NULL                         AND T00."TaxId4" <> '')               ELSE                      (SELECT LEFT(MAX(T00."TaxId0"), 10)                       FROM CRD7 T00                       WHERE T00."CardCode" NOT LIKE 'CL%'                         AND T0."CardCode"= T00."CardCode"                         AND T00."TaxId0" IS NOT NULL                         AND T00."TaxId0" <> '')           END AS "IDENTIFICAÇÃO",           T0."UserSign",           T0."U_NAME",           T0."BPLName",           T0."BPLId",           'NOTA FISCAL DE ENTRADA' AS "Tipo de documento" ,           T0."PARCEIRO CONSOLIDADO"    FROM CTE T0), PEDIDO_DE_COMPRA AS (SELECT T0."DocNum",           T0."DocDate",           T0."DocTotal",           T0."Serial",           T0."CardCode",           T0."Comments",       (SELECT MAX(T00."DocEntry")       FROM OPOR T00       LEFT JOIN POR12 T01 ON T01."DocEntry"= T00."DocEntry"       WHERE T00."CardCode"= T0."CardCode") AS "Nota mais recente",           T0."UserSign",           T3."U_NAME",           T4."BPLName",           T4."BPLId",           'NOTA FISCAL DE ENTRADA' AS "Pedido de compra" ,           T1."FatherCard" AS "PARCEIRO CONSOLIDADO"    FROM OPOR T0    LEFT JOIN OCRD T1 ON T0."CardCode" = T1."CardCode"    INNER JOIN POR12 T2 ON T0."DocEntry" = T2."DocEntry"    INNER JOIN OUSR T3 ON T0."UserSign" = T3."USERID"    INNER JOIN OBPL T4 ON T0."BPLId" = T4."BPLId"    WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N'  AND T0."DocStatus" = 'O'      AND T0."DocDate">=[%1]      AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2]),PEDIDO_COMPRA_2 AS   (SELECT T0."DocNum",           T0."DocDate",           T0."DocTotal",           T0."Serial",           T0."CardCode",           T0."Comments",                   AND T00."TaxId4" <> '')               ELSE                      (SELECT LEFT(MAX(T00."TaxId0"), 10)                       FROM CRD7 T00                       WHERE T00."CardCode" NOT LIKE 'CL%'                         AND T0."CardCode"= T00."CardCode"                         AND T00."TaxId0" IS NOT NULL                         AND T00."TaxId0" <> '')           END AS "IDENTIFICAÇÃO",           T0."UserSign",           T0."U_NAME",           T0."BPLName",           T0."BPLId",           'PEDIDO DE COMPRA' AS "NOTA FISCAL DE ENTRADA",           T0."PARCEIRO CONSOLIDADO"    FROM PEDIDO_DE_COMPRA T0), RECEBIMENTO AS (SELECT T0."DocNum",           T0."DocDate",           T0."DocTotal",           T0."Serial",           T0."CardCode",           T0."Comments",       (SELECT MAX(T00."DocEntry")       FROM OPOR T00       LEFT JOIN POR12 T01 ON T01."DocEntry"= T00."DocEntry"       WHERE T00."CardCode"= T0."CardCode") AS "Nota mais recente",           T0."UserSign",           T3."U_NAME",           T4."BPLName",           T4."BPLId",           'RECEBIMENTO' AS "RECEBIMENTO" ,           T1."FatherCard" AS "PARCEIRO CONSOLIDADO"    FROM OPDN T0    LEFT JOIN OCRD T1 ON T0."CardCode" = T1."CardCode"    INNER JOIN PDN12 T2 ON T0."DocEntry" = T2."DocEntry"    INNER JOIN OUSR T3 ON T0."UserSign" = T3."USERID"    INNER JOIN OBPL T4 ON T0."BPLId" = T4."BPLId"     WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocStatus" = 'O'      AND T0."DocDate">=[%1]      AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2]), RECEBIMENTO_2 AS   (SELECT T0."DocNum",           T0."DocDate", lançamento",T0."DocTotal" AS "Total do documento",T0."Serial" AS "Nº de série",T0."CardCode" AS "Código do cliente/fornecedor" ,T0."Comments" AS "Observações",T0."IDENTIFICAÇÃO",T0."UserSign" AS "Assinatura do usuário",T0."U_NAME" AS "Nome do usuário",T0."BPLName" AS "Nome da filial",T0."BPLId" AS "Filial",T0."Tipo de documento",T0."PARCEIRO CONSOLIDADO",        T0."Serial"||'-'||T0."IDENTIFICAÇÃO" AS "CHAVE-PRIMARIA" FROM CTE2 T0  UNION ALL   SELECT *,        T0."DocNum"||'-'||T0."IDENTIFICAÇÃO" AS "CHAVE-PRIMARIA" FROM PEDIDO_COMPRA_2  T0  UNION ALL   SELECT *,        T0."Serial"||'-'||T0."IDENTIFICAÇÃO" AS "CHAVE-PRIMARIA" FROM RECEBIMENTO_2 T0;

-- - Título: Relatorio financeiro de faturamento ROTAS CEASA - (0165)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio financeiro de faturamento rotas ceasa - (0165).
with CTE2 as (SELECT  T0."U_WB_RouteNumber", T3."Name", T0."DocTotal", T0."CardCode", T0."U_TX_DtSaid", T0."DocNum"   FROM OINV T0   INNER JOIN INV1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OCRD T2 ON T0."CardCode" = T2."CardCode" LEFT JOIN "@SD_ROTA" T3 ON T3."Code" = T0."U_WB_RouteNumber" WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T3."Name" LIKE '%%CEASA%%'  AND T1."Usage" =15 AND T0."CardCode" NOT IN ('CL001471','CL001482','CL001520','CL002158','CL003964','CL001264') AND T0."U_TX_DtSaid" >=[%1] and T0."U_TX_DtSaid"<=[%2] ), VALOR_NOTA AS (      SELECT DISTINCT T0."DocNum",T0."DocTotal",T0."U_WB_RouteNumber",T0."U_TX_DtSaid" FROM  CTE2   T0  ), VALOR_NOTA_LIQUIDO_CONSOLIDADO AS (     SELECT SUM(T0."DocTotal") AS "VALOR R$",T0."U_WB_RouteNumber",T0."U_TX_DtSaid" FROM  VALOR_NOTA T0 GROUP BY T0."U_WB_RouteNumber",T0."U_TX_DtSaid"  )    SELECT  T0."U_WB_RouteNumber" AS "Codigo da rota", T0."Name" AS "Nome da rota", (SELECT SUM(T00."VALOR R$") FROM VALOR_NOTA_LIQUIDO_CONSOLIDADO T00 WHERE T00."U_TX_DtSaid"= T0."U_TX_DtSaid" AND T0."U_WB_RouteNumber" = T00."U_WB_RouteNumber") as "VALOR LIQUIDO R$", T0."U_TX_DtSaid", (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT T00."CardCode") FROM CTE2 T00 WHERE T00."U_WB_RouteNumber" IN (T0."U_WB_RouteNumber") AND T0."U_TX_DtSaid" = T00."U_TX_DtSaid") AS "QUANTIDADE DE LOJAS NA ROTA", (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT T00."DocNum") FROM CTE2 T00 WHERE T00."U_WB_RouteNumber" IN (T0."U_WB_RouteNumber") AND T0."U_TX_DtSaid" = T00."U_TX_DtSaid") AS "QUANTIDADE DE NOTAS NA ROTA"  FROM CTE2 T0 GROUP BY  T0."U_WB_RouteNumber", T0."Name", T0."U_TX_DtSaid";

-- - Título: Relatorio notas canceladas  (PE) - (0202)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio notas canceladas  (pe) - (0202).
SELECT T0."DocNum", T0."BPLName",t0."UpdateDate",T0."DocDate" FROM OINV T0 WHERE T0."CANCELED" IN ('Y') AND T0."UpdateDate" >= [%1]   AND T0."UpdateDate" <= [%2]   AND T0."BPLName" IN ('JFC PRODUTOS AGRICOLAS', 'PE_MANOEL FERNANDO MORGADO CAMPANHA');

-- - Título: Relatorio notas canceladas (Sem PE) - (0201)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio notas canceladas (sem pe) - (0201).
SELECT T0."DocNum", T0."BPLName",t0."UpdateDate",T0."DocDate" FROM OINV T0 WHERE T0."CANCELED" IN ('Y')   AND T0."UpdateDate" >= [%1]   AND T0."UpdateDate" <= [%2]   AND T0."BPLName" NOT IN ('JFC PRODUTOS AGRICOLAS', 'PE_MANOEL FERNANDO MORGADO CAMPANHA');

-- - Título: Relatorio notas de entrada mp-produtor-rural - (0229)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio notas de entrada mp-produtor-rural - (0229).
SELECT distinct T0."DocEntry", T0."DocNum", T0."DocDate", T0."DocDueDate", T0."CardCode", T0."CardName", T0."BPLName", T0."DocTotal", T0."Comments", T0."WTSum"  FROM OPCH T0  INNER JOIN PCH1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  LEFT JOIN OCRD T2 ON T2."CardCode" = T0."CardCode" WHERE T0."CANCELED"='N' AND T0."DocDate" >=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%4] AND T2."GroupCode" =104 AND T0."BPLName" = [%5];

-- - Título: Relatorio para de consumo de itens acabados, produtos bases e alternativos OPEN (MP) - (0108)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatorio para de consumo de itens acabados, produtos bases e alternativos open (mp) - (0108).
with CTE  AS (SELECT T0."Code" as "Codigo Produto acabado", T2."ItemName" as "Descrição produto acabado", (SELECT SUM(T01."Quantity")   FROM OINV T00 INNER JOIN INV1 T01 ON T01."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry" WHERE T00."CANCELED" = 'N' AND T01."Usage" in (15) AND T00."BPLId" in(3) and T01."ItemCode" = T0."Code" AND T00."DocDate">= [%1] AND T00."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T00."CardCode" NOT IN ('CL001471','CL001482','CL001520','CL002158','CL003964','CL001264')) AS "Quantidade venda",'Item' as "Tipo de item", T1."Code" , T1."ItemName",T4."ItmsGrpNam" AS "Grupo de itens",  T1."Quantity",CASE WHEN T1."Type" = 290 THEN  T5."UnitOfMsr" ELSE T3."InvntryUom" END AS "Unidade de medida", T3."NumInBuy" as "Multiplo de compra", (SELECT SUM(T01."Quantity")   FROM OPCH T00 INNER JOIN PCH1 T01 ON T01."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry" WHERE T00."CANCELED" = 'N' AND T01."Usage" in (19,47) AND T00."BPLId" in (3) and T01."ItemCode" = T1."Code" and T00."DocDate">= [%1] AND T00."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T00."CardCode" NOT IN ('FO001340','FO002947','FO002087')) As "Quantidade de compra"  FROM OITT T0  INNER JOIN ITT1 T1 ON T0."Code" = T1."Father"  LEFT JOIN OITM T2 ON T2."ItemCode" = T0."Code" LEFT JOIN OITM T3 ON T3."ItemCode" = T1."Code" LEFT JOIN OITB T4 ON  T3."ItmsGrpCod" = T4."ItmsGrpCod" LEFT JOIN ORSC T5 ON  T5."VisResCode" = T1."Code"    WHERE T4."ItmsGrpCod" IN (119,120,121,122,123,124,125,131,137) and T0."Code" in ('00018-001','00253-001','00764-028','003582','003226','002770','002763','002775') ORDER BY T0."Code",T1."Type"),  CTE2  AS (SELECT T0."Code" as "Codigo Produto acabado", T2."ItemName" as "Descrição produto acabado", (SELECT SUM(T01."Quantity")   FROM OINV T00 INNER JOIN INV1 T01 ON T01."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry" WHERE T00."CANCELED" = 'N' AND T01."Usage" in (15) AND T00."BPLId" in(3) and T01."ItemCode" = T0."Code" AND T00."DocDate">= [%1] AND T00."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T00."CardCode" NOT IN ('CL001471','CL001482','CL001520','CL002158','CL003964','CL001264')) AS "Quantidade venda",'Item' as "Tipo de item", T6."AltItem" AS "Code", T7."ItemName",T4."ItmsGrpNam" AS "Grupo de itens",  T1."Quantity",CASE WHEN T1."Type" = 290 THEN  T5."UnitOfMsr" ELSE T3."InvntryUom" END AS "Unidade de medida", T7."NumInBuy" as "Multiplo de compra",(((SELECT SUM(T01."Quantity")   FROM OPCH T00 INNER JOIN PCH1 T01 ON T01."DocEntry" = T00."DocEntry" WHERE T00."CANCELED" = 'N' AND T01."Usage" in (19,47) AND T00."BPLId" in (3) and T01."ItemCode" = T7."ItemCode" and T00."DocDate">= [%1] AND T00."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T00."CardCode" NOT IN ('FO001340','FO002947','FO002087')) * T6."Match")/100)As "Quantidade de compra"  FROM OITT T0  INNER JOIN ITT1 T1 ON T0."Code" = T1."Father"  LEFT JOIN OITM T2 ON T2."ItemCode" = T0."Code" LEFT JOIN OITM T3 ON T3."ItemCode" = T1."Code" LEFT JOIN OITB T4 ON  T3."ItmsGrpCod" = T4."ItmsGrpCod" LEFT JOIN ORSC T5 ON  T5."VisResCode" = T1."Code" LEFT JOIN OALI T6 ON T6."OrigItem" = T1."Code" LEFT JOIN OITM T7 ON T6."AltItem" = T7."ItemCode"   WHERE T4."ItmsGrpCod" IN (119,120,121,122,123,124,125,131,137) and T0."Code" in ('00018-001','00253-001','00764-028') AND T6."OrigItem" is not null ORDER BY T0."Code",T1."Type")   SELECT *, (T0."Quantidade de compra" * T0."Multiplo de compra") as "Quantidade comprada na unidade de estoque", (T0."Quantidade venda" *  T0."Quantity") as "Quantidade necessária, baseado no produto acabado",( (T0."Quantidade venda" *  T0."Quantity")/4 ) as "Quantidade necessária por semana", (select  SUM(T02."OnHand") - SUM (T02."IsCommited") from   OITM T01  LEFT JOIN OITW T02 ON T02."ItemCode" = T01."ItemCode" where T0."Code" =T01."ItemCode" and T02."WhsCode" LIKE '03%%' ) AS  "TOTAL DISPONIVEL PARA BAIXA", (SELECT sum(T01."OpenQty") FROM OPOR T00 INNER JOIN POR1 T01 ON T01."DocEntry"  = T00."DocEntry" WHERE T0."Code" = T01."ItemCode" AND T00."DocDate"<current_date AND  T00."DocDate">= add_days(current_date,-30)) as "QUANTIDADE EM ABERTA PEDIDOS DE COMPRA 30 DIAS"   FROM CTE  T0   union all  select *,(T0."Quantidade de compra" * T0."Multiplo de compra") as "Quantidade comprada na unidade de estoque", (T0."Quantidade venda" *  T0."Quantity") as "Quantidade necessária, baseado no produto acabado",( (T0."Quantidade venda" *  T0."Quantity")/4 ) as "Quantidade necessária por semana", (select SUM(T02."OnHand") - SUM (T02."IsCommited") from OITM T01  LEFT JOIN OITW T02 ON T02."ItemCode" = T01."ItemCode" where T0."Code" =T01."ItemCode" and T02."WhsCode" LIKE '03%%') as "TOTAL DISPONIVEL PARA BAIXA", (SELECT sum(T01."OpenQty") FROM OPOR T00 INNER JOIN POR1 T01 ON T01."DocEntry"  = T00."DocEntry" WHERE T0."Code" = T01."ItemCode" AND T00."DocDate"<current_date AND  T00."DocDate">= add_days(current_date,-30)) as "QUANTIDADE EM ABERTA PEDIDOS DE COMPRA 30 DIAS"   from CTE2 T0  ORDER BY T0."Descrição produto acabado";

-- - Título: Relatório com notas baixadas no sistema - (0200)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatório com notas baixadas no sistema - (0200).
with cte as (SELECT    case when T1."InvType" = 14 then    (SELECT T10."DocNum"  FROM ORIN T10 WHERE T10."DocEntry"= T1."DocEntry") WHEN T1."InvType" = 30 then (select T13."TransId" from OJDT T13 WHERE T13."TransId" = T1."DocEntry") ELSE    (Select T11."DocNum"  from OINV T11 WHERE T11."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry") end as "Nro_Doc"     FROM ORCT T0  LEFT JOIN RCT2 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocNum"        WHERE T0."Canceled" = 'N'  AND T0."UpdateDate" >=[%1] AND T1."InvType"  = 13), CTE2 AS( SELECT  case when  T1."SrcObjTyp" = 13 THEN (SELECT T0."DocNum" FROM OINV T0 WHERE T0."DocEntry" = T1."SrcObjAbs") when T1."SrcObjTyp" = 14  then (SELECT T0."DocNum" FROM ORIN T0 WHERE T0."DocEntry" = T1."SrcObjAbs")  END AS "Nro do doc"    FROM OITR T0   INNER JOIN ITR1 T1 ON T0."ReconNum" = T1."ReconNum"  LEFT JOIN OCRD T2 on t2."CardCode" = T1."ShortName"    WHERE T0."CreateDate">=[%1]  AND  T1."SrcObjTyp" = 13 and T0."Canceled" ='N' AND T0."ReconType"  = 0 ), CTE3 AS (  SELECT  T0."Nro_Doc", CASE WHEN  (SELECT T00."DocStatus" FROM OINV T00 WHERE T00."DocNum" =T0."Nro_Doc")  ='O' THEN 'PAGO PARCIAL' ELSE 'FECHADO' END AS "Status_Doc" FROM cte T0  UNION ALL   SELECT *, CASE WHEN (SELECT T00."DocStatus" FROM OINV T00 WHERE T00."DocNum" = T0."Nro do doc") = 'O' THEN 'PAGO PARCIAL' ELSE 'FECHADO' END AS "Status"   FROM CTE2 T0)  SELECT DISTINCT * FROM CTE3;

-- - Título: Relatório consolidado de MP de Teresópolis por mês - (0210)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatório consolidado de mp de teresópolis por mês - (0210).
SELECT      TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocDate", 'MM-YYYY') AS "Mes",     T1."ItemCode",     T1."Dscription",     SUM(T1."Quantity") AS "Total_Quantity",     T2."BuyUnitMsr",     T3."ItmsGrpNam" FROM      OPCH T0       INNER JOIN PCH1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"     INNER JOIN OITM T2 ON T1."ItemCode" = T2."ItemCode"     INNER JOIN OITB T3 ON T2."ItmsGrpCod" = T3."ItmsGrpCod" WHERE      T0."DocDate" >= [%0]      AND T0."DocDate" <= [%1]      AND T2."ItmsGrpCod" IN (119, 122, 123, 131)      AND T0."BPLId" IN (3, 4, 6)      AND T0."CANCELED" = 'N'     AND NOT T0."CardCode"  IN ('CL002158', 'FO001424', 'CL001520', 'FO002947', 'CL001471', 'FO001340', 'FO000382', 'CL001482', 'FO001108', 'FO002087')       AND T1."Usage"<> 50 GROUP BY      TO_VARCHAR(T0."DocDate", 'MM-YYYY'),     T1."ItemCode",     T1."Dscription",     T2."BuyUnitMsr",     T3."ItmsGrpNam" ORDER BY      MIN(T0."DocDate"),     T1."ItemCode";

-- - Título: Relatório consolidado para apuração de pedido, recebimento, NF (MP) - (0173)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatório consolidado para apuração de pedido, recebimento, nf (mp) - (0173).
WITH PEDIDOS_COMPRA AS ( SELECT  DISTINCT  T0."DocDate",Count(Distinct T0."DocEntry") as "Quantidade de pedidos", SUM(T1."LineTotal")  as "VALOR PEDIDOS R$", T0."BPLName"  FROM OPOR T0 INNER JOIN POR1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OITM T2 ON T2."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode" WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T1."Usage" in (19,47) and T2."ItmsGrpCod" IN (119,120,121,122,123,124,125,131,137) AND T0."U_NotaAjusteInterno" = 'N'  GROUP BY  T0."DocDate", T0."BPLName" ), RECEBIMENTOS AS ( SELECT DISTINCT T0."DocDate",Count(Distinct T0."DocEntry") as "Quantidade de recebimentos", SUM(T1."LineTotal") as "VALOR RECEBIMENTO R$", T0."BPLName"  FROM OPDN T0 INNER JOIN PDN1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OITM T2 ON T2."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode" WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T1."Usage" in (19,47) and T2."ItmsGrpCod" IN (119,120,121,122,123,124,125,131,137) AND T0."U_NotaAjusteInterno" = 'N'  GROUP BY  T0."DocDate", T0."BPLName" ), NOTA_FISCAL_ENTRADA AS ( SELECT DISTINCT T0."DocDate",Count(Distinct T0."DocEntry") as "Quantidade de notas de entrada", SUM(T1."LineTotal") as "VALOR NOTA FISCAL DE ENTRADA$", T0."BPLName"  FROM OPCH T0 INNER JOIN PCH1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OITM T2 ON T2."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode" WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T1."Usage" in (19,47) and T2."ItmsGrpCod" IN (119,120,121,122,123,124,125,131,137) AND T0."U_NotaAjusteInterno" = 'N'  GROUP BY  T0."DocDate", T0."BPLName" ),  NOTA_FISCAL_ENTRADA_POR_DATA_DOCUMENTO AS ( SELECT DISTINCT T0."TaxDate",Count(Distinct T0."DocEntry") as "Quantidade de notas de entrada documento", SUM(T1."LineTotal") as "VALOR NOTA FISCAL DE ENTRADA_DATA_DOCUMENTO$", T0."BPLName"  FROM OPCH T0 INNER JOIN PCH1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OITM T2 ON T2."ItemCode" = T1."ItemCode" WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T0."TaxDate">=[%1] AND T0."TaxDate"<=[%2] AND T1."Usage" in (19,47)   and T2."ItmsGrpCod" IN (119,120,121,122,123,124,125,131,137) AND T0."U_NotaAjusteInterno" = 'N'  GROUP BY  T0."TaxDate", T0."BPLName" ),NumberSequence AS (     SELECT 0 AS N FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 1 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 2 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 3 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 4 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 5 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 6 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 7 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 8 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 9 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 10 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 11 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 12 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 13 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 14 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 15 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 16 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 17 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 18 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 19 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 20 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 21 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 22 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 23 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 24 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 25 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 26 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 27 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 28 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 29 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 30 FROM DUMMY     UNION ALL     SELECT 31 FROM DUMMY ), DATA_FINAL AS ( SELECT ADD_DAYS([%2],-DAYOFMONTH([%2]) + 1 + N.N) AS "Datas" FROM NumberSequence N WHERE ADD_DAYS([%2], -DAYOFMONTH([%2]) + 1 + N.N) <= LAST_DAY([%2]) ), EMPRESAS AS ( SELECT T0."BPLName"  FROM OBPL T0 WHERE T0."BPLId" <>2  )  SELECT    T0."Datas",  T1."Quantidade de pedidos", T1."VALOR PEDIDOS R$", T2."Quantidade de recebimentos", T2."VALOR RECEBIMENTO R$", T3."Quantidade de notas de entrada", T3."VALOR NOTA FISCAL DE ENTRADA$",T4."Quantidade de notas de entrada documento", T4."VALOR NOTA FISCAL DE ENTRADA_DATA_DOCUMENTO$", T5."BPLName"  FROM "DATA_FINAL" T0  CROSS JOIN EMPRESAS T5  LEFT JOIN PEDIDOS_COMPRA T1 ON T1."DocDate" = T0."Datas" AND T5."BPLName" = T1."BPLName" LEFT JOIN RECEBIMENTOS T2 ON T2."DocDate" = T0."Datas" AND T5."BPLName" = T2."BPLName" LEFT JOIN NOTA_FISCAL_ENTRADA T3 ON T3."DocDate" = T0."Datas" AND T5."BPLName" = T3."BPLName" LEFT JOIN NOTA_FISCAL_ENTRADA_POR_DATA_DOCUMENTO T4 ON T4."TaxDate"= T0."Datas" AND T5."BPLName" = T4."BPLName";

-- - Título: Relatório consolidado por rede, tipos de nota, supervisor, gerente e filial - (0114)
-- - Consulta - Esta consulta exibe os detalhes de: relatório consolidado por rede, tipos de nota, supervisor, gerente e filial - (0114).
SELECT T2."CardCode", T2."CardName", TO_VARCHAR(T2."AliasName") as "Nome fantasia",T5."Code", T5."Name", T7."State", SUM (T1."LineTotal") as "Valor R$", T6."BPLId", T6."BPLName", 'Nota de saída' as "Tipo de nota",T3."SlpCode", T3."SlpName",T4."AgentCode", T4."AgentName" FROM OINV T0   INNER JOIN INV1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OCRD T2 ON T0."CardCode" = T2."CardCode"  LEFT JOIN OSLP T3 ON T3."SlpCode" = T2."SlpCode" LEFT JOIN OAGP T4 ON T4."AgentCode" = T2."AgentCode" LEFT JOIN "@SD_CADREDE" T5 ON T5."Code" = T2."U_SD_Rede" LEFT JOIN OBPL T6 ON T6."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" LEFT JOIN INV12 T7 ON T7."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry"   WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' and T1."Usage" = 15 and t0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."CardCode" NOT IN ('CL001471','CL001482','CL001520','CL002158','CL003964','CL001264')   GROUP BY T2."CardCode", T2."CardName",TO_VARCHAR(T2."AliasName"), T5."Code", T5."Name", T6."BPLId", T6."BPLName",T3."SlpCode", T3."SlpName",T4."AgentCode", T4."AgentName",T7."State"  UNION ALL  SELECT T2."CardCode", T2."CardName",TO_VARCHAR(T2."AliasName") as "Nome fantasia",T5."Code", T5."Name", T7."State", -SUM (T1."LineTotal") as "Valor R$", T6."BPLId", T6."BPLName", 'Nota de devolução' as "Tipo de nota",T3."SlpCode", T3."SlpName",T4."AgentCode", T4."AgentName" FROM ORIN T0   INNER JOIN RIN1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OCRD T2 ON T0."CardCode" = T2."CardCode"  LEFT JOIN OSLP T3 ON T3."SlpCode" = T2."SlpCode" LEFT JOIN OAGP T4 ON T4."AgentCode" = T2."AgentCode" LEFT JOIN "@SD_CADREDE" T5 ON T5."Code" = T2."U_SD_Rede" LEFT JOIN OBPL T6 ON T6."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" LEFT JOIN RIN12 T7 ON T7."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry"   WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' and T1."Usage" in (15,38) and t0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."CardCode" NOT IN ('CL001471','CL001482','CL001520','CL002158','CL003964','CL001264')   GROUP BY  T2."CardCode", T2."CardName",TO_VARCHAR(T2."AliasName"),T5."Code", T5."Name", T6."BPLId", T6."BPLName",T3."SlpCode", T3."SlpName",T4."AgentCode", T4."AgentName",T7."State"  UNION ALL  SELECT T2."CardCode", T2."CardName",TO_VARCHAR(T2."AliasName") as "Nome fantasia",T5."Code", T5."Name", T7."State", -SUM (T1."LineTotal") as "Valor R$", T6."BPLId", T6."BPLName", 'Nota de devolução paga' as "Tipo de nota",T3."SlpCode", T3."SlpName",T4."AgentCode", T4."AgentName" FROM OPCH T0   INNER JOIN PCH1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry"  INNER JOIN OCRD T2 ON T0."CardCode" = T2."CardCode"  LEFT JOIN OSLP T3 ON T3."SlpCode" = T2."SlpCode" LEFT JOIN OAGP T4 ON T4."AgentCode" = T2."AgentCode" LEFT JOIN "@SD_CADREDE" T5 ON T5."Code" = T2."U_SD_Rede" LEFT JOIN OBPL T6 ON T6."BPLId" = T0."BPLId" LEFT JOIN PCH12 T7 ON T7."DocEntry" = T0."DocEntry"    WHERE T0."CANCELED" ='N' and T1."Usage" = 50 and t0."DocDate">=[%1] AND T0."DocDate"<=[%2] AND T0."CardCode" NOT IN ('FO001340','FO002947','FO002087')   GROUP BY T2."CardCode", T2."CardName",TO_VARCHAR(T2."AliasName"), T5."Code", T5."Name", T6."BPLId", T6."BPLName",T3."SlpCode", T3."SlpName",T4."AgentCode", T4."AgentName",T7."State";

-- - Título: Relatório de acordo de desconto de produtor - (0268)

SELECT T3."BPLName",T1."ItemCode", T1."Dscription", T0."DocNum",T0."DocDate", T2."CardCode", T2."CardName",T0."Serial",T0."PaidToDate" AS "Saldo utilizado" ,CASE WHEN T0."DocStatus"  ='O' THEN 'ABERTO' ELSE 'FECHADO' END AS STATUS, T0."DocTotal", T0."Comments" FROM ORPC T0  INNER JOIN RPC1 T1 ON T0."DocEntry" = T1."DocEntry" INNER JOIN OCRD T2 ON T0."CardCode" = T2."CardCode"  LEFT JOIN OBPL T3 ON T3."BPLId" = T0."BPLId"  WHERE T1."ItemCode" = '007405' AND T0."CANCELED" ='N' AND T3."BPLName" = [%2];

-- - Título: Relatório de apuração de quebra por boleto - (0164)

T2."Serial",(T2."DocTotal"+T2."DiscSum") as "Total do documento",T2."DocTotal" as "Total liquido", T2."DiscSum", T2."DiscPrcnt",T1."ReconSum" AS "SALDO UTILIZADO", CASE WHEN T0."ReconType"  IN (0,4) THEN 'RECONCILIACAO MANUAL'  WHEN T0."ReconType"  =3 THEN 'BAIXA CR' END AS "TIPO DE BAIXA", T7."ValueDocument" as "Valor boleto individual",T12."ValueDocument" AS "Valor boleto agrupado", T7."OurNumber",T12."OurNumber",T9."Description" as "Status boleto individual",T13."Description" AS "Status boleto agrupado",T11."DicountValue",T11."InstallmentValue", T11."DicountValue", T11."InstallmentValue",  CASE WHEN T7."ValueDocument" >0 THEN ((T2."DocTotal"+T2."DiscSum") - T7."ValueDocument") ELSE (T2."DocTotal"+T2."DiscSum") - T11."InstallmentValue" END AS "DIFERENÇA", case when  (T9."Description" <>'Cancelado' and T9."Description" is not null  and T13."Description" = 'Cancelado' or T13."Description" is null ) then T7."OurNumber" when T13."Description" <>'Cancelado' and T13."Description" is not null then T12."OurNumber" end as   "Nro Boleto",case when  (T9."Description" <>'Cancelado' and T9."Description" is not null  and T13."Description" = 'Cancelado' or T13."Description" is null ) then  T7."DateCreate" when T13."Description" <>'Cancelado' and T13."Description" is not null then T12."DateCreate" END  as "Data de criação do boleto no SAP", T2."FatherCard"   FROM OINV T2  LEFT OUTER  JOIN ITR1 T1 ON  (T1."SrcObjAbs" = T2."DocEntry" AND T1."SrcObjTyp" = 13)   LEFT OUTER  JOIN  OITR T0 ON T0."ReconNum" = T1."ReconNum" LEFT JOIN OCRD T4 ON T4."CardCode" = T2."CardCode"  LEFT JOIN "@SD_CADREDE" T6 ON T4."U_SD_Rede" = T6."Code"   LEFT OUTER  JOIN "IntegrationBank"."IV_IB_BillOfExchangeInstallment" T11 ON T2."DocEntry" = T11."DocEntry"   LEFT OUTER  JOIN "IntegrationBank"."IV_IB_BillOfExchange"  T12 ON T11."BoeId" = T12."ID"   LEFT OUTER  JOIN "IntegrationBank"."IV_IB_BoeStatus" T13 ON T12."Status" = T13."ID" AND T13."Description" <>'Cancelado' LEFT OUTER  JOIN "IntegrationBank"."IV_IB_BillOfExchangeSituation" T14 ON T14."ID" = T12."Situation"  LEFT OUTER  JOIN "IntegrationBank"."IV_IB_BillOfExchange" T7 ON T2."DocEntry" = T7."DocEntry"   LEFT OUTER  JOIN "IntegrationBank"."IV_IB_BoeStatus" T9 ON T7."Status" = T9."ID" AND T9."Description" <>'Cancelado' LEFT OUTER  JOIN "IntegrationBank"."IV_IB_BillOfExchangeSituation" T10 ON T10."ID" = T7."Situation"   WHERE  (((T0."Canceled" = 'N' OR T0."Canceled" IS NULL ) AND (T2."CANCELED" = 'N')) AND (T2."BPLId" NOT IN (5))  AND  (T1."SrcObjTyp" =13 OR T0."ReconNum" IS NULL))  AND (T13."Description" is not null OR T9."Description" is not null ) AND (T0."ReconType"  IN (13,4,3,0) OR T0."ReconNum" IS NULL )  AND    (MONTH(TO_DATE(T7."DateCreate")) >= MONTH((SELECT MIN(T0."ReconDate")  FROM OITR T0  INNER JOIN ITR1 T1 ON T0."ReconNum" = T1."ReconNum"   LEFT JOIN ORIN T2 ON T1."SrcObjAbs" = T2."DocEntry" LEFT JOIN OCRD T4 ON T4."CardCode" = T2."CardCode" LEFT >=[%1] AND T0."ReconDate"<=[%2])) OR  MONTH(TO_DATE(T12."DateCreate")) >= MONTH((SELECT MIN(T0."ReconDate")  FROM OITR T0  INNER JOIN ITR1 T1 ON T0."ReconNum" = T1."ReconNum"   LEFT JOIN ORIN T2 ON
